Madrid: A correspondent from this newspaper has sent news from the front lines of the Guadarrama Mountains, stating that the situation on the front lines did not change much last night. Government troops are still working to consolidate their positions and prepare for an attack. The rebels fired their cannons more frequently yesterday, but the government troops' positions were not damaged. Another batch of security forces arrived at the front lines last night. The government here has recently issued several orders: (1) Declaring Huelva Province, Cadiz Province, the Balearic Islands, Lugo Province, Corunna Province, and Pontevedra Province as war zones. (2) Assigning the Canary Islands (in the Atlantic Ocean), Ifni (south of German Morocco), and Rio de Oro (i.e., the desert area of Spanish Morocco) to the jurisdiction of the "Governor-General of Morocco." (3) The governors of the three provinces of Santander, Toledo, and Murcia have all been dismissed and replaced with new personnel. (Havas Telegram, 11th)

Government Declares Military Progress on All Fronts, Victory in Cordoba Province 23

Madrid: Interior Minister Pozas recently declared that government troops have made progress on all front lines yesterday. The most notable is on the southern front in Cordoba Province. After several fierce battles, the government troops have occupied the village of Adamuz, from which they can drive straight down, and the city of Cordoba can be obtained easily. The situation in the capital is very peaceful, and people are working as usual. "The number of militiamen is currently sufficient for deployment, but when necessary, everyone should take up arms to defend the country and either annihilate the enemy or die on the battlefield." Madrid: The Ministry of the Army recently announced that government troops have occupied the village of Adamuz in Cordoba Province in the south. Subsequently, the government troops advanced and occupied the villages and towns north and south of Huesca. The city of Huesca will be taken soon. (Havas Telegram, 11th)

Rebel Forces Grow Stronger Day by Day, Battle Line Runs From South to North Across the Country 24

Pamplona: Regarding the military situation, former Minister of Justice Escobedo recently told a reporter from this newspaper that the current battle line between the revolutionary army and the government army starts from Carvajales in the far north, bordering France (on the southern slopes of the Pyrenees). From there, it runs south through the city of Huesca, the city of Zaragoza, turns southwest through the city of Daroca, turns west through the city of Sigüenza (at the eastern end of the Guadarrama Mountains), the city of Atienza (in the middle of the Guadarrama Mountains), crosses the Guadarrama Mountains through the city of Segovia (on the northern foothills of the Guadarrama Mountains), and turns southwest through the city of Ávila (west of the city of Madrid), the city of Plasencia, until the city of Cáceres (not far from the Portuguese border). Then it turns south through the city of Badajoz, and then turns southeast to the port of Malaga on the Mediterranean coast. This battle line runs from north to south across the country. The government army controls the east side, while the revolutionary army controls the west side. However, the northwest corner along the Bay of Biscay, from the city of Oviedo in the west (in Asturias Province) to the city of Fuenterrabía in the east (at the western end of the Pyrenees Mountains, where France and Spain meet), the area (west of the aforementioned battle line) is currently occupied by the government army. In addition, the southern province of Granada (east of the aforementioned battle line) is still in the hands of the revolutionary army. Both places are exceptions, protruding into the other side's positions. (Havas Telegram, 10th)

Frequent Reports of Foreign Nationals Killed 25

(Rome) Regarding the case of the killing of Italian nationals in Barcelona, Spain, official sources recently stated that the situation has become quite serious since this case occurred. The government initially did not want to make an issue of it, so as not to increase the tension. Therefore, although it has protested to the Spanish government, the nature of the protest is ordinary and only requested compensation, without any implication of an ultimatum. Moreover, other foreign nationals have also been killed in this Spanish unrest, not just Italian people. Italy does not intend to take a special attitude. (Havas Telegram, 10th)

The government of the Argentine capital recently received a report from its embassy in Spain that four nationals have been killed in Madrid. The government immediately protested to the Spanish government. The Spanish government stated in its reply that it has strictly ordered the military and police to properly protect the Argentine embassy and nationals. (Agence Havas Telegram, 11th)

(London) British national Captain Savile was sailing on the yacht "Blue Shadow I" when it was shelled by the Spanish rebel cruiser "Cervera." Savile died on the spot, and his wife was also seriously injured. This accident is directly attributed to the rebel cruiser "Cervera." The Spanish authorities in Gibraltar have expressed their condolences to the British government. Mrs. Savile is currently recuperating in a hospital in Saint-Jean-de-Luz. According to reports, her condition is good and she is expected to recover within days. Both of Mrs. Savile's legs were injured by shrapnel. The "Blue Shadow" was shelled because it was mistaken for a ship belonging to the Spanish government. (Reuters Telegram, 10th)

Spanish Rebel Policy: Republic or Monarchy Undecided 26

Lisbon: A local newspaper today published an interview with General Franco, the leader of the Spanish rebels, stating that Madrid, the Spanish capital, is now under tight siege, and the residents of the city are forced by hunger and will force the government to surrender. When asked whether the Spanish flag used by the Northern Army was a republican flag or a monarchist flag, Franco replied that the republican flag is currently the official flag of the revolution, but the issue will be discussed later. (Reuters Telegram, 11th)

Lisbon: General Franco, the leader of the rebels, stated today when meeting with visitors that if they win, the new Spain will be governed according to the corporatist system, or according to the same principles of nation-building as Portugal, Italy, and Germany. Once they have completely occupied Spain, all citizens who have joined the revolutionary army and collaborated in resisting the government must disarm and will no longer participate in political affairs. General Franco declared that the revolutionary army will definitely win, saying that the Madrid authorities have prepared everything, and will abandon the capital as soon as the revolutionary army begins to advance. Moroccan Rebel Headquarters: Another Twenty-One Airplanes Arrive; German Airplane Detained in Spain; Italy Expresses Approval on Non-Intervention Issue; Britain and France in Contact, Hoping to Establish Agreement Soon 27

Twenty-one airplanes recently flew into the port of Tangier, destined for Tetouan, the stronghold of the Spanish Moroccan rebels. According to the rebel staff headquarters, these airplanes are owned by Spain itself and not supplied by foreign countries. It was also reported that several Germans in plainclothes were seen busying themselves at the rebel headquarters, and there were more native soldiers in the streets of Tetouan than usual. (Havas, 10th)

(London) The arrival of twenty-one airplanes at the Spanish rebel headquarters in Tetouan on Sunday has raised suspicions. A Roman official spokesman stated today that the claim that the planes departed from the Vorticello airfield near Rome is false. However, according to news received from Tangier in Paris, the arrival of the planes has been confirmed by the rebel headquarters in Tetouan, but rebel leaders claim that the planes all belong to the Spanish government. (Reuters, 11th)

After a German Junkers airplane was detained yesterday in Archaga, north of Seville, it was learned today that four more Junkers airplanes, which were prepared to transport German nationals out of the country, have also been detained. It is reported that they were seized by government troops in the Badajoz region. The German Embassy has not yet commented on this matter, only denying that the German airplane detained yesterday in Archaga was piloted by Germans. (National News Agency, 10th)

Madrid reports that a German Junkers three-engine bomber landed near the city of Barajas on the 9th of this month. On the same day, it flew to the western border province of Badajoz and landed in Archaga, where it was seized by government air forces. The plane carried three German pilots and one Spaniard. It is said that they believed that General Mola, commander of the northern rebel forces, had already occupied the capital, so they landed near the capital. Upon learning that this was incorrect, they resumed flight, but were forced to land in Archaga due to running out of fuel. Prime Minister Quiroga recently told the press that the government will thoroughly investigate this matter, and that he is increasingly optimistic about the general situation of the war. (Havas, 11th)

(Berlin) It was officially announced today that the Spanish government has detained several airplanes belonging to the German Lufthansa airline. These airplanes were intended to evacuate German nationals seeking refuge in Madrid. It was also announced that, if necessary, Germany will send the torpedo boats "Kondor" and "Mowe" to Spain to protect the safety of German nationals and their repatriation. Currently, 4,130 German nationals have been evacuated from Spain, but 1,400 remain, of whom over 300 are unwilling to leave Spain due to economic reasons. (Reuters, 10th)

Madrid: The Spanish government forces have transported the German airplane that was forced to land in Badajoz to this city. The airplane is marked with the number 52 and bears the Nazi swastika symbol. However, it was not armed. It is said that the three Germans and one Spaniard on board have been arrested. (National News Agency, 10th)

(Paris) According to Le Figaro, eight fighter planes and six twin-engine airplanes flew from near Toulouse in southern France to an unknown destination. Each plane was reportedly equipped with eight machine guns. The newspaper said that a large number of Spanish aviation personnel were present when the airplanes departed. (National News Agency, 11th)

(Paris) Italian Foreign Minister Ciano yesterday delivered the Italian government's response to the French draft of the non-intervention agreement to French Ambassador Chambrun. According to well-informed sources, the content of the Italian response is more favorable than predicted by the Italian newspapers. Italy has accepted the French proposal and has put forward the following two measures for consideration: (1) Prohibition of financial assistance to the warring factions in Spain; (2) Prohibition of citizens of all countries from volunteering to serve in either of the warring factions. (Havas, 11th)

(London) The Italian government's reply states that it agrees in principle with the French proposal, but with certain reservations. The points that the Italian government still needs to discuss with the French government will not be disclosed at this time to facilitate diplomatic negotiations between the two countries. (Reuters, 11th)

(London) Today, reliable sources here report that France intends to invite the United States to join the European countries' non-intervention agreement regarding the Spanish Civil War. It is said that German Foreign Minister Neurath stated in a note sent to Britain and France on Saturday that Germany, while agreeing in principle to this neutrality agreement, believes that it must include the United States to be effective. (National News Agency, 10th)

(London) According to responsible sources, the British Ambassador to Germany, Sir Eric Phipps, was instructed on Saturday to visit the German Foreign Office to support the French request for non-intervention in the Spanish Civil War. At that time, the German Foreign Office argued that the United States should also be invited to join this non-intervention agreement. Political figures believe that the United States would not find it difficult to join due to its current Neutrality Act. It is also reported that the German government also put forward opinions on the method of monitoring the implementation of the non-intervention agreement (one of the three issues raised by Italy) and argued that the citizens of all countries who volunteer to serve in the warring factions in Spain, as well as private donations to aid the warring factions, should be prohibited. (Havas, 10th)

(London) The British and French governments are currently in close contact regarding the French initiative for a non-intervention agreement among various countries regarding the Spanish Civil War. Britain is very welcoming of this matter and has already informed the governments of various countries. France is keeping the British authorities informed of the progress of this matter at all times. It is also reported that the news received from various parties suggests that the French proposal to prohibit the sale of arms, ammunition, and airplanes to any side in Spain has been supported by various countries. Although there are still several points that need to be negotiated, the major concerned countries are on the verge of reaching an agreement in principle. The difficulty felt by several governments is that their aspirations seem to go further than the French proposal. Britain believes that after the agreement is signed, any shortcomings can be added later. The primary concern of all relevant countries at present should be to avoid the dangers of the situation, and the first priority is non-intervention. It is important not to sacrifice practical results by being overly perfectionist. It is hoped that the major governments involved will issue a declaration in accordance with the French proposal as soon as possible, without delay. (Reuters, 11th)

London: The French Chargé d'Affaires in Britain recently consulted with Sir Mounsey, an expert from the Foreign Office, on the implementation measures of the non-intervention agreement in the Spanish Civil War. According to political figures, the British government will take appropriate measures to prevent the transit of foreign arms to Spain. These measures must not conflict with existing British law to avoid amending the law. Political figures also stated that there are currently two main difficulties regarding the draft non-intervention agreement: one is that the Italian government has not yet made a clear statement, and the other is that Portugal requires all countries to guarantee its borders. Regarding the former, Italian Prime Minister Mussolini returned to Rome from his villa in the Province of Forlì last night to take charge, and the Italian response is expected to be sent out tomorrow. Regarding the latter, the government will declare to Portugal that, in the event of an incident, Britain is prepared to fulfill the obligations stipulated in the Anglo-Portuguese Treaty of 1810 and the League of Nations Covenant. In addition, Britain will also argue that even if a radical leftist regime is established in Spain, the threat to Portugal should not be greater than the establishment of a fascist or quasi-fascist regime. It is expected that the Portuguese government will accept Britain's views. Currently, the Soviet Union and the Scandinavian countries have accepted the French proposal, which is very gratifying to political figures, who stated that Britain will instruct its ambassadors abroad to actively engage with the relevant countries to support the French proposal so that the non-intervention agreement can be successfully concluded as soon as possible. (Havas, 10th)

(Paris) Regarding the draft agreement on non-intervention in the Spanish Civil War, responsible sources have learned that the Soviet government has given its unreserved support. It has already implemented a ban on the shipment of all military supplies, including military and commercial airplanes, to Spain, as proposed by France. However, regarding the clause in the preamble of the draft stating that each signatory country is willing to maintain strict neutrality, it is proposed that it should be deleted. Since the Italian government has distinguished between the terms "neutrality" and "non-intervention," different interpretations of this statement in the preamble will inevitably arise among various countries. Some countries may believe that this is a permanent recognition of the Spanish government forces and the rebel forces as equal belligerent parties, while other countries only recognize the Madrid government as the legitimate government recognized by the powers. If so, obstacles will inevitably arise in future negotiations, and every effort should be made to avoid this. Responsible sources here state that the French government has no objection to the Soviet views. (Havas, 10th)

(London) Regarding the French request to conclude a non-intervention agreement in the Spanish Civil War, only Portugal has not yet responded. It is reported that the Portuguese government intends to put forward the following three reservations: (1) The neutral status of the port of Tangier in North Africa must be respected by both warring parties in Spain; (2) The Soviet Union must accept the non-intervention agreement at the same time as other countries; (3) Britain and France must guarantee the territorial integrity of Portugal (referring to the threat to Portugal's security if communism spreads within Spain, leading to a state of anarchy). Regarding the third condition, people here generally say that Britain's obligation to guarantee Portugal's territorial integrity is clearly stipulated in the Anglo-Portuguese Treaty of 1810 (during the Napoleonic Wars, Britain and Portugal were allies). This treaty is based on the Anglo-Portuguese Treaty of 1703 (during the War of the Spanish Succession in 1703, Britain and Portugal were also allies, standing against France and Spain). The two are in the same vein, with the same purpose, and the treaty of 1810 is still valid today, with its contents unchanged. According to Article 1 of the Anglo-Portuguese Treaty of Friendship, this friendship treaty and the defensive alliance relationship between the two signatory countries, and their close, inviolable, and linked relationship, shall be permanent, firm, and unchangeable, so as to ensure public security, maintain common interests, and when any enemy attacks one of the signatory countries, the two countries shall mutually guarantee to defend it. Article 2 stipulates that if any of the two signatory countries of Britain and Portugal is threatened by an attack from another country, then the other signatory country shall do its utmost to either prevent the outbreak of war or enable the threatened country to obtain fair and complete satisfaction. Britain's obligations are very clear, as can be seen from this. (Havas, 10th)

New German Ambassador to Britain 29

(Berlin) The German Ambassador to Britain, Herr Hoesch, passed away in office several months ago. The vacant position has now been filled by General Ribbentrop, appointed by Führer Hitler. Ribbentrop is a trusted confidant of Führer Hitler. He represented the Führer in Britain to negotiate disarmament issues and signed the Anglo-German Naval Agreement in London in June last year. After Germany declared the abolition of the Locarno Treaty in March of this year, he went to London again to attend the extraordinary meeting of the Council of the League of Nations, where his efforts in negotiations were highly commendable. (Vossische Zeitung, 11th)

(Berlin) Hitler has appointed his special envoy, General Ribbentrop, as the ambassador to Britain, a position previously held by Dr. Hoesch, who died suddenly in London. Ribbentrop's appointment is welcomed by London political circles because he has many friends in London. Ribbentrop is familiar with the nature and habits of the British people, and it is expected that he will be able to perform his duties satisfactorily. Ribbentrop has visited Britain frequently in recent years, which is why he was honored with this position, so that British and German opinions can become closer. The establishment of the Anglo-German Naval Agreement is almost entirely due to Ribbentrop's efforts. After taking office, Ribbentrop will make it his main goal to enhance the friendship between Britain and Germany. Ribbentrop is 43 years old and joined the Nazi Party only four years ago. During these four years, he served as a commissioner on disarmament issues and then as Hitler's plenipotentiary envoy. Ribbentrop is the son of a military man and is particularly known for his proficiency in several languages. (Reuters, 11th)

It is reported that the plan drafted by Zou, Song, and Tang focuses on unifying the legal tender system, stabilizing Guangdong's finances, and protecting the interests of Guangdong currency holders, and will set a discount rate between Guangdong currency and legal tender. (Central News Agency, 11th)

Beining Railway's Smuggling Sharply Reduced Compared to Before 39

(Tianjin) According to relevant sources, the smuggled goods transported to Tianjin by the Beining Railway have been sharply reduced compared to before, with only about 10 tons per day. The types of goods are mainly hardware and seafood. Artificial silk and foreign sugar are rarely seen these days. The goods transported by rail to various places are mostly diverted to the Ping-Sui Railway for sales due to the strict inspections on the Ping-Han and Jin-Pu lines. (Central News Agency, 11th)

(Tianjin) For several days, the goods declared for transit to the Tianjin East General Station have mostly been perfume, rouge, alcohol, foreign wine, and kerosene. The customs has been striving to simplify the declaration procedures for the convenience of merchants, and the procedure to inspect goods transported by rail requires obtaining an inspection form from the freight station, having it stamped by the customs, and then handing it over to the railway station for loading. On the night of the 10th, 200 bags of sugar, over 100 reams of cigarette paper, and 300 boxes of kerosene were transported from Nandasi to Tianjin. Recently, Japanese are actively seeking sales markets in the Ping-Sui Railway. The private goods transported daily through Tianjin to Fengtai and Zhangjiakou are gradually increasing. (Special Dispatch, 11th)

(Tianjin) Regarding the conflict between the Tianjin suburban tax police and a Japanese merchant over the seizure of smuggled tobacco, the Japanese consul submitted a written protest to the customs on the 11th, still pointing to the insult to the national flag, but the customs has no responsibility for this. (Special Dispatch, 11th)

(Tianjin) Smuggled goods transported via the South Canal have not been smuggled on the Jin-Pu Railway for three weeks. The Dongzong and Liangzhan stations are reporting 400 pieces of normal local goods in transit every day, twice as many as before. The customs believes that the transport of goods by the Jin-Pu Railway will return to normal within half a month. (Special Dispatch, 11th)

Huaxin Yarn Factory Renamed Gongda No. 7 Factory; Scheduled to Start Work on September 6; Draft Agreement Signed Between China and Japan 40

(Tianjin) The Huaxin Yarn Factory sold to the Japanese Kanegafuchi Spinning Company is scheduled to start work on September 6. A draft agreement has been signed between the two parties. The representatives of Huaxin are directors Liu Junqing and Xu Jishang, and lawyer Lin Xinggui. The Japanese representative is Kanegafuchi director Kurachi. After the start of work, it will be renamed Gongda No. 7 Factory. The draft agreement states: (1) A deposit of 100,000 yuan will be paid from the date of signing; (2) The remaining 1.1 million yuan will be paid in one lump sum upon entering the factory; (3) The existing cotton yarn and other goods will be paid in cash at discounted prices by the new factory; (4) All factory employees will be continued for three months, and all workers will be continued for six months; (5) This draft agreement is valid from the date of signing. The new owner plans to suspend work for five days starting on September 1 to handle the handover and liquidation procedures. Kurachi has inspected the factory with technicians on the 11th and gave instructions on everything. Tianjin Yuyuan was also bought by Kanegafuchi Spinning Company, becoming Gongda No. 6 Factory. With the purchase of Huaxin, it has already established a foundation in the North China spinning industry. (Special Dispatch, 11th)

(Shenyang) Traffic on the North Manchurian Railway to Manchouli is currently interrupted due to continuous rain and rising river waters, which have washed away two sections of the line. The committee resolved to publish the main points of each case as follows: (1) Regarding the request for interpretation from the Xiamen Kulangsu Chinese Assembly, (a) should citizens who have previously taken the oath of registration in this island take the oath again this time, and (b) since there are no township or neighborhood chiefs or joint guarantee leaders in this island, can the election of candidates be carried out by a vote of twenty councilors at a meeting? (2) The Zhejiang Provincial Government telegraphed to inquire whether the district chiefs of the first, second, and third districts in Hangzhou City, where there are no township or neighborhood chiefs and no Baojia system, can elect candidates. (3) The Shanghai Election Supervisor inquired whether the Shanghai Municipal Council, together with the Shanghai Municipal Party Department, could be considered as the corresponding personnel to exercise the right of election, based on the situation in the city. The above three cases were discussed together and resolved as follows: (1) Based on the number of citizens who have taken the oath, temporary election areas should be divided, and one person should be designated as a neighborhood chief. The corresponding personnel may be designated by the municipal government to fill the position. (4) Wu Guozhen, the mayor of Hankou, telegraphed to request clarification on whether store members can participate in occupational elections. Resolved: According to the precedents set by the National Assembly, they are allowed to participate in the election as representatives of the members. (6) For lawyers' associations that adopt a committee system, should the executive committee members who jointly elect candidates be limited to standing committee members? Resolved: Limited to standing committee members. (7) Regarding the calculation of the number of votes for candidates in Article 12 of the Implementing Rules, should the votes be calculated separately by county or combined? Resolved: The number of votes for candidates should be calculated separately for each county. (Central News Agency dispatch, 11th)

A House Collapse Tragedy Occurred in Suzhou 54

(Suzhou) At around 11:00 PM, at the Lu Shude Tang Chinese medicine shop in Lianxi Fang in the city, many people were enjoying the cool air on the platform along the river due to the hot weather. Neighbors and police officers rushed to the scene upon hearing the sound and tried to rescue them, but three people had already drowned. Seven people were rescued, and the young owner is missing. It is not yet known whether he drowned. The other seven rescued people are also in critical condition and are being treated in the hospital. (Special dispatch, 11th)

Overview of the Puppet Troops in Chahar North: Troops Entirely Commanded and Trained by a Certain Country; Politics Also Controlled by Special Service Chiefs 56

Zhangjiakou Correspondence: Since the puppet troops occupied Chahar North, all news has been extremely suppressed. Travelers are subject to inspection, making it difficult for outsiders to understand the truth. Recently, a person from Chahar North spoke in detail about the current situation and the organization of the local garrison. A brief account of the military and political situation is as follows:

Military

Li Shouxin, the commander of the Puppet Inner Mongolia First Army, is in his forties and is a Mongolian from Rehe Province. He was a former subordinate of Cui Yuwu. During the September 18th Incident, he followed Commander Cui in resisting the Japanese around Lingyuan, Rehe, enduring many hardships. Later, as the situation changed, and under Japanese and puppet pressure, Commander Cui went into retirement, while Li surrendered to the puppet regime with his troops. Most of his subordinates are from Rehe Province. After occupying Duolun, his strength was still 4,000 strong. After several rounds of downsizing by the puppet army, only 2,000 remained, organized into two brigades and one regiment. The first brigade commander is a Mr. Liu, the second brigade commander is a Mr. Yin, and the artillery regiment commander is a Mr. Ding. At that time, they were closely monitored and harshly treated, and the officers and soldiers were willing to revolt. Since the unit advanced to Zhangbei last winter, discipline has been stricter than before, and the puppet side does not seem as harsh as in the past. It was expanded into an army. The third brigade (commander Mr. Wang) is still short of personnel and is currently stationed in Baochang and Zhanyuan areas. The unit's firearms are quite well-equipped, entirely new guns made by Han Linchun (approximately 3,000), and the salaries of officers and soldiers have also increased accordingly. Recently, the puppet side also appointed Li as the mayor of Dehua City (i.e., Huade County), so Li travels back and forth between Zhangbei and Dehua. The puppet side attaches great importance to his military strength, but it is only 3,000 cavalry, 13 artillery pieces, and 8 machine guns. The command and training of the unit are entirely directed by people from a certain country. The first brigade commander, Mr. Liu, is from Shandong and was also a former subordinate of Cui Xingwu. He is extremely loyal and very obedient. He constantly laments the weakness of the motherland. Most of his subordinates are also from Rehe Province. His political skills are also very sharp. He has now been appointed by the puppet side as the garrison commander of Zhangbei, with the brigade headquarters located in Zhangbei. The first regiment is stationed in the Dahulun Baochang area, the second regiment is stationed in the Nanhaoqian Tumu Road (under Zhangbei jurisdiction), and the third regiment is stationed in Zhangbei city. The second brigade commander, Yin Baoshan, is fifty years old, from Rehe, and was also a former subordinate of Cui Xingwu. He is treacherous and has close ties with the puppet side. His troops are stationed in Shangdu, Shangyi, and Kangbao. The third brigade commander, Mr. Wang, has troops currently in the Guyuan and Duolun areas. It is rumored that they are miscellaneous troops from northern Yanqing who were reorganized by him. The artillery regiment commander, Mr. Ding, is thirty-two years old, from Rehe, and is currently stationed outside the west gate of Zhangbei. In addition, there are communications companies, special detachments, and other organizations, all stationed in Zhangbei city.

Yu Ziqian, the commander of the Puppet Border Self-Government Army, is in his forties and from Suiyuan. He previously served as a bureaucrat in the Suiyuan Provincial Public Security Bureau. This spring, he used local autonomy as a slogan and traveled between Zhangbei and Suiyuan. Due to secret contacts with a certain high-ranking military officer of the puppet side, he recruited unemployed military personnel and local self-defense bandits from Sui Province. The gathering place is in the Dahushan area of Qijia Village, Sanbaogou, Er District, Zhangbei (Suiyuan border). There are currently five to six hundred people, with only two to three hundred guns. Recently, after a roll call by a person from a certain country, only 100 shi of millet was issued. The local area has suffered greatly. They are currently awaiting reorganization.

Jin Jiasan, the commander-in-chief of the Puppet Xingya Joint Army Group, is from Fengtian. He previously served as a brigade commander in the Sixty-third Army under Feng Zhanhai. Lin Zhuxuan, the puppet deputy commander, is in his forties, from Lishu County, Fengtian. Zhang Songtao, the current director of the General Affairs Section of Zhangbei County, is thirty-nine years old, from Hebei, and is also a puppet deputy commander. On July 20th, Jin, Lin, and their entourage of more than thirty people secretly went to Zhangbei. Currently, only the name of the army group exists; no soldiers or staff have been seen. It is rumored that they have reached an agreement with the head of a certain country's agency in Beiping. After many days of deliberation, they have contacted the troops in northern Rehe and the border areas, as well as miscellaneous troops. They will soon gather in Chahar North. The number of people is more than other units. The puppet side has agreed to completely incorporate private guns and self-defense group guns in Chahar North. Whether this will become a reality is still uncertain.

Bao Dele'e, the commander of the Puppet Inner Mongolia Second Army, is in his thirties and is a Mongolian from Rehe Province. His team of 1,800 people was newly recruited in Rehe and is currently stationed in the Gonghui Town, San District, Zhangbei County. The puppet side is actively training them, but discipline is not very strict and firearms are not complete. They will not be a major threat in the future.

Wang Daoyi, the commander of the Puppet Northwest Anti-Communist Army, recently organized the Puppet Northwest Anti-Communist Army with the head of a special service agency from a certain country stationed in Dehua. His troops are the bandits of Lv Erxiao. In mid-July, they began to gather in the villages of Erquan Jing Sanyi City in the Third District of Zhangbei. With no food or pay, the local area is completely responsible for their supplies. Robberies occur several times a day, and the population has fled. Due to the unbearable harassment, gentry, merchants, and civilians have requested to be moved to the Shangyi area for reorganization. It is rumored that they will soon be moved to the Shangdu County border to carry out disturbances on the Suiyuan border. As for the number of people, there are 2,200, with 600 horses and 1,200 guns.

Wang Youji, the commander of the Puppet Independent Division, is in his twenties and currently works as a section member in the Puppet Mongolian Public Office. He was an instructor during the incident. He is currently engaging in activities to win over local respected but frustrated military personnel and is planning to organize the Puppet Independent Division, operating in the Haoqian area. He has already gathered more than 200 people.

Bu, the principal of the Puppet Youth School, is a Mongolian, currently forty years old, and serves as the head of the Mongolian Section of the Education Department in the Puppet Mongolian Office. This spring, the school was established, gathering more than 300 Mongolian youth from the twelve banners of Chahar League. People from a certain country serve as instructors.

Political

Zhuo Te Bazhabu is the League Chief of Chahar League, with the League Chief's Office located in Zhangbei County. Under the League, there are three departments: General Affairs, Education, and Security, governing the eight counties of Chahar North (Chahar North originally had six counties, but recently the puppet army divided the three administrations of Shangyi, Huade, and Chongli into counties). Guyuan was merged into another county. The military and political powers of the banner are also controlled by the head of a special service agency from a certain country. Huade County in Chahar North, formerly Jiabusi, was renamed Huade County not long after the incident. Recently, it was renamed Dehua City, not belonging to the Chahar League. Guyuan County, due to insufficient revenue, was merged into Duolun and Baochang counties. The Baochang County Government was renamed Baoyuan County. (8th)

Typhoon Sweeps Through Chaoshan; Mountain Torrents Erupt in the Fujian-Jiangxi Border Region; Extremely Heavy Losses in Chaozhou and Meizhou Counties 57

Shantou Correspondence: Thirteen years ago, Chaoshan experienced a "8-2" typhoon disaster. Coastal villages and fishing boats were wiped out, with tens of thousands of deaths. Civil agricultural losses exceeded tens of millions. Transportation in various places only returned to normal half a month later. The streets of Shantou City turned into a field of silt and rubble. Corpses floated everywhere in the sugarcane fields of Chenghai and Raoping. The stench lingered for several days. People of Chaozhou still shudder at the thought. However, on the eve of "8-2" this month, i.e., August 1st, the Customs had already hoisted a hurricane signal. Scheduled ships to various ports were all stopped in the harbor to shelter from the wind, not daring to sail, numbering more than ten ships. Ferries, fishing boats, etc., terrified by the lingering power of the "8-2" typhoon, hid in the harbor in advance. From the 1st, strong winds and heavy rain raged, with the wind speed traveling at 150-160 miles per hour, heading straight inland to the Fujian-Jiangxi border. The coastal counties are plains, and most of the early rice has been harvested. As the typhoon arrived, the water level on the plains rose two to three feet. Boats sailed on land in various villages, and many highway bridges were damaged. The Chaoshan Railway and the embankment highway were also damaged, making them impassable. By the 2nd, the wind was even more intense, continuing all day. Land and water transportation between Shantou and various counties was completely suspended. Telegraph poles and wires were destroyed in many places, and news was disrupted. On the coast, giant waves were like mountains, with the force of ten thousand horses galloping and drums beating. When the sea waves hit, the water spray rose dozens of feet high. Various cargo store entrances hurriedly lowered floodgates, using cement to seal the door gaps and sewers. In the streets, roof tiles, door and window glass fragments flew in the air due to the wind, falling with the rain, making a crashing sound. Countless pedestrians and rickshaw pullers were struck, their heads broken and bleeding. The terrain below Qilu in Shantou City is like a pot, and the water flooded into people's homes two to three feet deep. Many houses had their tiles lifted by the wind, and the rainwater poured into the houses. A ship from Siam went to Shantou, and a small boat went to pick up passengers, causing two boat capsizings and eleven deaths. No boat dared to sail out to sea heart again after that. On the evening of the 2nd, mountain torrents erupted in Fujian and Jiangxi, pouring down from the Meixian and Dapu rivers, flowing straight into Chaoan City. In less than an hour, the water level on the Xiangzi Bridge rose two zhang. Shopkeepers on the bridge almost could not move away in time. When the flood came, the foam on the wave head was seven or eight feet higher than the water surface, like white silk and city walls, rolling out from the villages, all the people's belongings, such as rice straw, cow sheds, bamboo baskets, water tanks, wooden benches, wooden beds, shoes, clogs, clothing trunks, wooden cabinets, white iron buckets, door panels, and even the thatched grass on the fields, were uprooted and rolled down. Bunches of hemp bamboo, thirty to fifty stalks, with green bamboo leaves, rolled down with the flowing water. There were also bamboo cradles, with months-old babies crying inside, the cradles like small boats, passing over the Xiangzi Bridge surface and heading out to sea. There were also cows, dogs, chicken coops, and chickens inside. All of this was seen after the flood had passed, showing the situation of people in the countryside being unable to escape from their dreams as the mountain water suddenly rose. Many things flowed out of the Han River, not stopping for three days, one pile after another, half floating and half sinking. Looking from the Chaoan city tower, half a li away from the river heart; everyone could not clearly see what was flowing down. On the evening of the 2nd, the strong wind and heavy rain did not stop. The river water had already risen to the outside of the East Gate of Chaozhou City. Each city gate lowered the wooden boards to prevent water, stacking as many as eight pieces. The water outside the gate submerged to the fifth piece. On the morning of the 3rd, the river water continued to rise by more than one zhang. At many places in the Han River and its tributaries, the dikes developed leaks and became dangerous. Responsible persons from the river management associations in each district and township patrolled the dikes day and night, ordering able-bodied men from nearby villages to prepare sack bags, fir wood, and sand to place near the dangerous dikes for rescue. In the afternoon, the river water was turbulent and gradually receding. All electric boats and sailing ships dared not set sail. On the morning of the 4th, the rain stopped and the wind subsided. According to telegrams from Songkou in Meixian and Sanheba in Dapu, heavy rain poured down, the sky was dark, and the river water continued to rise unabated. Because mountain torrents erupted in the Fujian-Jiangxi border region, the mountain water did not follow the old paths of streams and gullies, penetrating into people's homes and villages. The village ground and objects swept away by the water were all gone. All boats dared not go downstream, and highway cars were also suspended. On the 5th, the sky in Shantou had cleared, but the river water had not receded. The disaster situation upstream was more severe than expected in Chaozhou and Shantou.

National Conference on Child Welfare Concludes, All Proposals Passed, and Declaration Issued 58

Qingdao Correspondence: The Second National Conference on Child Welfare, which opened on the 4th of this month, held meetings for several consecutive days, with the 8th being the final day. The third plenary session began at 8:00 AM. After Chairman Cheng Guanyi reported, Ms. Wang Xiuying was invited to speak on "Observations and Thoughts on American Children's Education." This was followed by various review reports. Hu Zuyin, the head of the research group's review committee, reported on the pending proposals from yesterday (all passed). The head of the administrative group's review committee then reported on the results of the review (all passed). It was decided to convene the fourth plenary session. After a report by Madam Niu Huisheng, chair, Ms. Chen Yi was invited to speak on "The Family's Responsibility for Child Welfare Work." After the speech, the chair proposed an additional motion on "Preparations for Relief of Children During Extraordinary Times," which was handed over to the executive committee of the Child Welfare Association to formulate a concrete plan for effective implementation. Finally, the draft of the conference declaration was approved, and it was decided that the date of the next conference would not be fixed but would be convened when necessary. The meeting adjourned at 1:00 PM. At 5:00 PM, the closing ceremony was held, presided over by Qingdao Mayor Shen Honglie. After the chairman delivered the closing remarks, all representatives took an oath to show their solemnity. The conference declaration and the subsequently passed proposals are recorded below:

Conference Declaration

The enduring survival of the nation and the flourishing of the national spirit depend on the continuous efforts of generations of citizens to strive unceasingly. Modern citizens should not only inherit the endeavors of previous generations in seeking survival but must also lead the rising generations in preparing to shoulder significant missions. At this moment when we are united in striving for the revival of the national movement, we believe that educating modern children is the most important and urgent task. In a few years, the responsibility for maintaining the nation's life and promoting the national spirit will rest on the shoulders of today's children. Therefore, in the past two years, we have diligently worked according to the resolutions of the National Child Welfare Leadership Conference, not daring to slacken, hoping to fulfill our mission and realize the expectations of the people. Based on our experiences and observations over the past two years, we deeply understand that in these times of national hardship and economic distress, children not only need our proper education but also our widespread relief and effective protection. The National Government is the leading body for the revival of the nation, and therefore, it deeply understands the fundamental importance of child welfare for the revival of the nation and actively promotes it. Thus, last year, the Executive Yuan decided in its meeting that the 24th year of the Republic should be designated as Children's Year and organized the National Children's Year Implementation Committee, tasking it with planning and promoting practical methods for implementing child welfare and earnestly advocating implementation to raise national awareness of child welfare. Having pledged ourselves to child welfare as our vocation, we should act practically under the leadership of the government. As the National Children's Year comes to an end, we are holding the Second National Conference on Child Welfare in Qingdao to review the past and encourage the future. We also offer our humble opinions for the government's consideration. We have observed that the methods of children's education and all protection measures in modern countries around the world are becoming increasingly organized, widespread, and meticulous, constantly improving, all planned to enhance the nation and increase its power in the future. All members of this association hope that our government will have more progressive child-rearing policies and systematic organizations, issuing orders to provincial and municipal governments to plan, establish, or increase the number of nurseries in rural factories and other child welfare projects, and that all public and private universities nationwide will have social, family, psychological, and educational departments to study teaching methods and train specialized talents to cooperate with child welfare organizations. Furthermore, we hope that the China Child Welfare Association will be assisted so that it has sufficient power to specially hire experts in various fields to conduct research and experiments to guide the national child welfare cause, enlightening the people, so that the great cause of reviving the nation can continue to advance, and the national spirit can be promoted and enhanced. The convening of this conference is of such great significance, and the mission of the attending representatives is even more arduous. Therefore, this conference emphasizes the four words "Child Welfare Builds the Nation" as the guideline for our work. The resolutions of this conference should be handed over to the China Child Welfare Association for practical implementation. The children of today are the masters of the future nation. Whether the future nation is sound depends entirely on whether the children of today are sound. To make the children of today into sound citizens is to lead the future nation to a sound state. We should adhere to this principle and work diligently, day and night. This is our declaration.

Proposals Passed

(A) Administrative Group: (1) Proposal for Appropriation of Funds: Nine cases, including 2, 4, 5, 15, 12, 32, 36, 39, and 63, were reviewed together. Review comments: 1. For the request to allocate funds, the conference should submit a request to the central government to allocate funds and order provincial and municipal governments to appropriate a certain percentage of local revenue or disaster relief funds as special funds for child welfare. The original child welfare funds in the local area should be effectively reorganized to ensure practical use. 2. For the request to allocate funds from the Boxer Indemnity, continue the resolution of the First National Conference, and the conference should formulate a plan and resubmit the request. 3. For the request to allocate part of the inheritance tax, the conference should request the central government to allocate a certain percentage when levying the inheritance tax, to be distributed by the Child Welfare Association to various regions as special funds for child welfare, and request that all unclaimed inheritances be allocated to child welfare funds. 4. Regarding the proposal to include child welfare education expenses in the budget, the conference should request the central government to include child welfare education expenses when preparing the budget for the 26th year of the Republic. Resolution passed. (2) Proposal for Establishing Nurseries: Seven cases, including 6, 9, 17, 43, 60, 62, and 64, were reviewed together. Review comments: According to the resolution of the First National Conference, the conference should request the central government to urge provincial and municipal governments to proceed in stages according to local conditions. Passed. (3) Proposal for Developing the Association's Work and Ensuring that Provincial, Municipal, and County Organizations are United: Eleven cases, including 20, 24, 29, 30, 31, 34, 35, 46, 49, 50, were reviewed together. Review comments: The conference should formulate a plan for promotion and unification based on the methods in cases 1 and 6 of the administrative group of the First National Conference and implement it effectively. Passed. (4) Proposal to Exempt Legally Established Child Welfare Organizations from Real Estate Taxes: Three cases, including 8, 13, and 19, were reviewed together. Review comments: The conference should refer to the original regulations passed by the 258th meeting of the Executive Yuan and submit a request accordingly. Passed. (5) Proposal to Request the Government to Dispatch Specialists to Inspect and Guide Child Welfare Work: Five cases, including 14, 22, 26, 37, and 44, were reviewed together. Review comments: 1. Request the government to be responsible for inspecting and guiding child welfare work at all levels. 2. Request the central government and provincial and municipal governments to establish positions for specialized personnel to manage child welfare and children's education. Report the situation accordingly. Resolution passed. (6) Request the Government to Give Preferential Treatment to Poor Children in Child Welfare Organizations by Allowing Them to Attend School Free of Charge: Three cases, including 25, 27, and 61, were reviewed together. Review comments: Passed as is. (7) Request to Establish More Charitable Educational Institutions at All Levels: Review comments on cases 12, 18, 23, 35, 38, 55, and 56 reviewed together: A special committee should be established to formulate a plan for phased implementation based on the original proposal. Passed. (8) Proposal to Send Child Welfare Publications Immediately: Cases 28 and 42 were reviewed together and passed. (9) Proposal to Subsidize Child Welfare Organizations: Cases 7, 26, and 40 were reviewed together and passed. (10) Request the Government to Enact a Child Welfare Protection Law: Passed.

Songjiang: Kidnapping Case in Xiao Kunshan 59

Xiao Kunshan in the fourth district of the county is a place where rivers and streams are numerous, and cases of robbery and kidnapping occur from time to time, with Miaogang as the den. At about 10:00 PM the night before last, the four-year-old child Huoguan of farmer Fan Shuquan's family in Xijinggang Township was kidnapped. It was reported that seven bandits came that night, one of whom jumped in first with a bamboo pole, opened the main gate, and the bandits swarmed in, speaking in a local dialect, carrying hand torches and other equipment. The homeowner couple, hearing the noise, fled from the adjacent room, leaving behind their four-year-old child, who was lying in bed and could not be taken away in time. The bandits did not search for valuables but only took the child and left. Before leaving, they stole a small boat from the nearby Fan Shulou family and carried the child westward along the Liu River.

Suzhou: Investigation of the Disappearance of Patrol Officer 60

Ma Puzhen, a patrol officer of the Fourth Substation directly under the Dongting Sisong Township Public Security Bureau, suddenly disappeared less than ten days after taking office the previous month. At that time, the Public Security Bureau had no knowledge of it. It was not until more than twenty days had passed before Inspector Zhuang Hongji learned of the situation when he went to the township to investigate duty performance. He immediately reported to Director Zhang, who is now investigating the matter. However, the township is isolated on Tai Lake, and it is unknown whether there are other circumstances. Therefore, Chief Inspector Zhang has been specially dispatched to conduct a thorough investigation to clarify the truth. However, the patrol officer of the substation did not report the disappearance of Patrol Officer Ma for so long, which is highly inappropriate and will be subject to appropriate punishment.

Complaint of Soil Paste Shops to the Yuan Ministry 61

The county government was ordered to recover 70,000 yuan in illegal profits from privately increasing soil prices by the Rongtai and other three soil paste shops. It is now learned that the county government originally set a deadline of ten days. Therefore, on the 11th, it issued tickets to summon the managers of each soil paste shop to carry out the arrest and pursuit in order to enforce the provincial order. However, each soil paste shop believes that this increase in soil paste prices was approved by the County Opium Prohibition Conference and was not a private price increase. Therefore, they are unwilling to pay and have filed a complaint with the Yuan Ministry. On the one hand, they jointly submitted a report to the county government, requesting a temporary suspension of the arrest and pursuit before the complaint is adjudicated.

Qingpu: Theft from the Anting Town Office

The Anting Town Credit Cooperative, attached to the Anting Central Primary School, was burglarized on the night of July 13, with a loss of more than 2,000 yuan in funds and grain coupons. A hole was dug in the glass window on the side of the side room, and although the tin box was wide open, there were no signs of damage. Therefore, the cooperative's treasurer, Ma Haosheng, believed it was the work of an insider and reported it to the Xu Gongqiao Public Security Substation. When Branch Director Wang arrived at the scene to investigate, he immediately suspected Jin Wangchen, a teacher at the school. Unexpectedly, Jin is the brother-in-law of Ma Shujingxian. Ma Jingxian had previously won the first prize in a lottery in Shanghai last spring. He became arrogant and thought of covering up for his brother-in-law, so he indirectly implicated Qian Qinghe, a resident of Jiajie Town, as a suspect. He even led the Kunshan County police to search Qian's home across the border, but found nothing. It is said that Qian Qinghe has filed a lawsuit.

Wuxi: Hall Order to Investigate the Theft of Grain Certificates 62

Deng Jiqian, a certificate inspector at the County Government's Land Tax Office, reported that his son, Deng Haozhang, and certificate inspectors Zhou Yuedu, Zhou Xilun, Zhu Shuqing, Zhang Huisheng, Zhou Ruru, and six others had colluded to commit fraud and steal grain certificates. The county government summoned them one after another. In addition to Deng Haozhang and Zhou Yuedu, who were detained, the remaining four, including Zhou Xilun, were released on bail. County Magistrate Shan Long will submit a report to the Finance Department for review. Yesterday, the Finance Department issued an order as follows: (1) The county's certificate inspection work must be handled carefully and completed on schedule and reported for verification. (2) All suspects in the grain certificate theft case should be dismissed from their positions and provide a reliable guarantor. Those without a guarantor should be placed under surveillance and a list submitted for review. (3) The original informant should be strictly interrogated and monitored to prevent him from fleeing out of fear of punishment.

Changzhou: Sheng Shouchhen's Bigamy Involved in Litigation 63

Lv Ruizhi, the wife of Sheng Shouchhen, a prominent family in Wu Yi, is 45 years old and currently resides in the Lv residence on Shizi Street. Ruizhi married Shouchhen in March of the fourth year of the Republic. Unexpectedly, after Shouchhen's father, Ouling, passed away in September, Shouchhen frequently insulted Ruizhi. By the sixth year of the Republic, after suffering abuse, she became seriously ill and nearly died. She then sought refuge with her mother's family and lived there for several years. Later, Shouchhen left without saying goodbye, and his whereabouts were extremely secretive. Ruizhi was abandoned for more than ten years, hoping that Shouchhen would repent. However, recently, a relative showed her the Shanghai News from September 6 of the seventeenth year of the Republic, only then did she learn that Shouchhen had publicly entrusted lawyer Zhou Zhonghao to publish an announcement of his marriage to Zhang Ruoyu. It was also learned that his brother, Xunchen, as the head of the family, presided over the wedding. Ruizhi went to Shanghai to reason with them but to no avail. After returning to Changzhou, she hired lawyer Yun Kuiyao to file a lawsuit with the local prosecutor's office against Sheng Shouchhen, Zhang Ruoyu, and others for bigamy and abandonment. Shouchhen's brother, Xunchen, was accused of assisting in the bigamy. She requested that the case be heard and investigated in accordance with the law. The prosecutor's office held a court hearing on the 11th, which attracted unusual attention from local people, who went to inquire about the matter.

Changshu: Autumn Heat Damages Rice Fields 64

Since the beginning of summer, the weather here has been unevenly cool and hot, with more rain and a cooler climate. Unexpectedly, since the beginning of autumn, it has suddenly become extremely hot, with the thermometer suddenly rising to 97 or 98 degrees. As a result, seasonal epidemics have also become prevalent. Most frighteningly, the rice fields in various villages have suffered from this autumn heat. Black spike disease has been found in the Dayi Bridge and Wangzhuang areas in the west of the city. This type of black spike disease is highly infectious. Once the rice plants are steamed by the autumn sun, they turn black and die. Measures are currently being taken to eradicate it. As for the various agencies in the urban area, they have announced a three-day suspension of office work. If the heat continues, measures will be taken to extend the suspension.

Giant Robbery Case in Shanghu Solved 65

The Zhangmu Bridge near West Lake and the Hubin of Xieshuilubridge in this county have been repeatedly robbed by bandits, and homeowners have been killed or injured. It is now learned that the Second District Criminal Investigation Team of the Suzhou Public Security Bureau received a tip that a gang of bandits was hiding in Wei Jing Tang outside Qimen. They immediately dispatched personnel and arrested the gang leader Wang Dejin and Zhang Jinlong. Gu Xiaomanzi, Liang Luren, Liang Luxiang, and women Jiang and Jin were arrested at Taiping Bridge in Xiangcheng. After being detained by the bureau, they confessed to robbing Changshu Zhangjiadian, Zhangmu Bridge, the West Lake area, Suzhou Taiping Bridge, and Jiapu Bridge in Wujiang. They killed two homeowners, claiming that it was revenge in the Sanbaitang area of Tongli. They have now been transferred to the Second District Headquarters of the Water Police. The County Public Security Bureau, upon hearing the news, believed that the bandits had committed numerous crimes in Changshu and planned to send a document to Suzhou to bring the bandits back to Changshu for trial.

Nantong: Repair of the Zhiyun Pagoda on Wolf Mountain 66

Wolf Mountain in Nantong is one of the famous scenic spots on the Yangtze River. The Zhiyun Pagoda on it is a Song Dynasty building. Two years ago, it was damaged by lightning and fire. The abbots of the Baiyi Temple, Zhunti Temple, and Sanyuan Palace on the mountain, Zhiliang, Wei Yi, Canlian, and Huijun, went to Shanghai a few days ago to raise funds from various parties for repairs. With the advocacy of Zhu Ziqiao, Li Qiqing, Zhang Jingshen, Fei Fanjiu, Wang Xiangwu, Cao Xizhi, Zhang Zhenxi, and others, fellow Nantong villagers in Shanghai donated generously and have already collected a considerable amount. Architect Fan Wenzhao was specially invited to the mountain to survey and draw repair plans, and the Gu Shengji Construction Company was contracted to carry out the repairs. After signing the contract, the repair cost is estimated at 15,000 yuan, with one-third to be paid in advance. Construction will begin soon, with a deadline for completion. It is said that the top of the pagoda will be covered with glass tiles, which will be more luxurious and magnificent than before, and the top of the pagoda will also be fitted with colored electric torches. All ferries passing by at night can see the lighthouse from afar, adding a lot to the scenery of the river.

Jiaxing: Road Construction Incident Resolved 67

After the Hangzhou-Shan Road construction workers caused a disturbance in Puyuan Town, located at the junction of Jiaxing and Tongxiang, on the 8th, although the police team suppressed it, the road workers seized two guns and injured the team members, causing a strike by various shops (all within Tongxiang County). After the authorities of Tongxiang and Jiaxing counties arrived in Puyuan to investigate and persuaded the shops to open, the shops reopened on the 10th. Zhang Zhouwen, the county magistrate of Tongxiang, and Jiang Zhongfan, a staff officer of the Jiaxing District Headquarters, convened local agencies and representatives of France on the afternoon of the 10th and invited Zhou Ruilin, director of the Hangzhou-Shan Road Linjia Section Engineering Office, and the engineers of the Tongyuan Section to discuss and resolve: (1) Workers shall not enter residents' homes freely. (2) Workers should be issued identification marks. (3) Workers should pay cash for goods and must not force credit sales. (4) The eight workers involved in the incident who were arrested, including Zhou Yatou, will be sent to the county government for punishment, while the remaining eleven will be taken back by the contractors with guarantees. (5) The owners of He Xinji will be responsible for recovering and returning the two guns seized by the workers within a specified time.

The inspection procedures will be decided after arriving in Guangdong. He plans to stay in Guangdong for at most two or three weeks before returning north.

Ju's Remarks

President Ju also told a reporter from the Central News Agency at the scene that after arriving in Guangdong, he will inspect the recent judicial situation in Guangdong Province as a reference for future reforms. He does not plan to stay in Guangdong for long and will return north in two weeks. On the way back north, he will pass through Hong Kong to meet with Xiao Focheng, who is currently recuperating in Hong Kong, and urge Xiao to go north to Beijing as soon as possible to jointly manage national affairs. Foreign newspapers reported that after arriving in Guangdong, he would fly to Nanning to meet with Li Bai to mediate the situation in Guangxi, but this is not the case, and he has not heard of the central government having this decision. As for whether there have been telegrams between Nanjing, Lushan, and Guizhou recently to discuss resolving the situation in Guangxi, he does not know the details. According to his observation, the situation in Guangxi can be resolved peacefully to avoid armed conflict. The newly appointed Guangxi Pacification Director Huang Shaoxiong also plans to go to Guangzhou in the next few days. As for the issue of Chen Jitang's future, the central government seems to be able to give him a nominal position to go abroad for investigation.

商會檢私會　發表貨物運銷須知　分為洋貨土貨兩部　有關貨物共二十六 70

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, for the convenience of merchants in various industries regarding the transportation and sales of goods, yesterday had the Inspection Committee formulate "Guidelines for the Transportation and Sales of Goods During the Inspection Period," for relevant industries to request and consult at any time. The full text is recorded below: Guidelines for the Transportation and Sales of Goods During the Inspection Period. (A) Regarding the Portion of Imported Foreign Goods Stipulated by the Ministry: (1) All factories, businesses, transfer companies, etc., that sell, use, transfer, and transport goods that the Ministry of Finance stipulates should be inspected (attached) must first apply to the Customs for registration and a license. (Note) Violations of this provision will be subject to a fine of more than two hundred yuan but not more than five thousand yuan. (2) When applying to the Customs for registration, the business or company must be certified by the industry association. If there is no industry association certificate, the Chamber of Commerce can certify (factories can also be certified by the Federation of Factories) before the Customs will issue a license. (The Customs charges one national currency for each license issued.) (3) After the goods are imported, if they need to be transferred to various places for sale, you can present the tax payment certificate (commonly known as a pass) to the Customs and request a shipping and sales license before you can start transporting. (If transported by train, you must apply for a tax-paid road transportation certificate.) (4) The shipping and sales license obtained should be sent to the local industry association (or directly to the local Chamber of Commerce if there is no industry association) for storage and registration when the goods arrive at their destination. If you want to distribute to other places, you must report to the local industry association or Chamber of Commerce and request a distribution license. (Note) Violations of items three and four will be subject to a fine of up to 20% of the value of the goods transported. (5) The validity period of the shipping and sales license is determined by the Customs according to the distance of the journey. After the goods arrive at their destination, the industry association or Chamber of Commerce that stored the license will keep it and submit it to the issuing Customs on a monthly basis. As for the validity period of the distribution license, it is determined by the issuing industry association or Chamber of Commerce according to the distance of the journey. After the goods arrive, the original sender must mail it back to the issuing industry association or Chamber of Commerce within three days. (6) All businesses, factories, and transfer companies should prepare books to record the source, sales, storage, and transfer of imported goods separately, for the Customs or the agency designated by the Ministry of Finance to send personnel to inspect at any time. (Note) Violations will be subject to a fine of more than one hundred yuan but not more than three thousand yuan. (B) Regarding the Transportation and Sale of Domestic Goods: (1) When domestic goods pass through Customs, they should be reported to the Customs for a domestic goods transportation and sales license. If the goods still need to be transported to other places for distribution after arriving at their destination, the industry association or Chamber of Commerce should be notified to issue a domestic goods distribution license based on the domestic goods transportation and sales license issued by the Customs. (2) If domestic goods are transported inland without going through Customs, the industry association should be notified. If there is no industry association, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce should be notified to issue a domestic goods certificate. (3) When obtaining a transportation and sales license from Customs, you must first register with Customs and obtain a license. (C) List of Foreign Goods that Should Apply for a Transportation and Sales License: Rayon, alcohol, alcoholic liquors and beverages, such as whiskey, brandy, liqueur, gin, Japanese sake, various sweet wines, aniline dyes, dry batteries, rubber boots, canned food, cigarette paper, dried scallops, cosmetics and perfumes, electrical materials, needles, kerosene, diesel oil, various piece goods, rubber tires, rubber shoes, various dried seafood products, caustic soda, sugar.

為綢緞運銷問題　代表赴京請願　馮原料執照換疋頭執照　事實上綢緞將無法運銷 71

Regarding the Issue of Silk and Satin Transportation and Sales: Representatives Go to Beijing to Petition. The Raw Material License is to be exchanged for a Piece Goods License. In reality, silk and satin will not be able to be transported and sold.

The Municipal Silk and Satin Industry Association believes that according to the "Measures for Inspection and Clearance of Domestic Goods Piece Goods Woven with Rayon" promulgated by the Ministry of Finance, it is stipulated that a rayon transportation and sales license must be exchanged for a piece goods transportation and sales license. However, there are very few silk factories in our country that directly import raw materials and produce and sell themselves. Most silk and satin are transferred and sold to Shanghai by silk merchants and then distributed to various places. If the aforementioned regulations are followed, it will be impossible to transport and sell them. Therefore, the association resolved to send representatives Luo Qinghua, Xu Limin, Pan Runsheng, Wang Jiean, Wu Xingcha, and five others, accompanied by Jin Runxiang, standing committee member of the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, and Ge Jiec臣, director of the Inspection Committee, to go to Beijing. The representatives took the night train to Beijing yesterday. In addition to carrying a petition from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and the Silk and Satin Industry Association for a personal presentation, the Chamber of Commerce first telegraphed the Ministry of Finance to report the matter. The original telegram is as follows: To the esteemed Ministry of Finance in Nanjing: The domestic silk fabrics sold by the silk and satin industry in this city are purchased and resold from silk weaving factories and small-scale machine households. It is impossible to obtain tax receipts from rayon merchants to exchange for transportation licenses. This is the same as the inability of the domestic goods industry to obtain unified tax receipts from inland handloom households and the inability of confectionery merchants to obtain import tax receipts for foreign sugar. We have already submitted a detailed report to your ministry and requested that the domestic silk fabrics sold by the industry be allowed to be released along the way with a certificate from the industry association and exempted from submitting receipts for inspection. However, we have not received a reply, and the Customs and Railway Bureau are firmly enforcing the order, and the industry's freight transportation has come to a complete standstill. This is not beneficial to stopping smuggling, and it is extremely related to domestic silk merchants. The industry has sent representatives Luo Qinghua and five others to the ministry for a personal presentation. We request that the various items presented by Jiang Ri be quickly adopted and transferred for implementation. Sincerely, Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce.

The Jiangsu-Zhejiang Silk and Satin Weaving Federation believes that the recent "Measures for Inspection of Domestic Goods Piece Goods Woven with Rayon or Mixed with Rayon" promulgated by the Ministry of Finance pose many difficulties for the transportation and sale of silk and satin in the inland. Yesterday, Wang Jiean was specially appointed as a representative to carry a petition and took the Beijing-Shanghai night express train to Beijing at 12:00 last night to petition the Ministry of Finance and the Tax Department separately, requesting that a flexible approach be approved to facilitate transportation and sales and maintain domestic silk. We now present the association's petition as follows: To the esteemed Minister Kong of the Ministry of Finance in Nanjing and Director Gao of the Tax Department: We respectfully read the "Measures for Inspection and Clearance of Domestic Goods Piece Goods Woven with Rayon or Mixed with Rayon" promulgated by your ministry, which stipulates that a rayon transportation and sales license must be exchanged for the piece goods transportation and sales license. Although the original text refers to factories, it is found that there are not many silk factories in our country that directly import raw materials and weave and sell themselves. Most of the silk factories in Su, Hang, and Huzhou are family industries and small-scale silk production, which are transferred and sold to Shanghai by silk merchants and then distributed to various places. If the aforementioned regulations are followed, it will be impossible to transport and sell them, which will greatly hinder domestic goods. The association believes that imported rayon and imported foreign silk piece goods should be handled with transportation licenses and distribution orders. As for the domestic silk piece goods woven in the inland areas of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, they should be certified by the local industry association and then allowed to be distributed to various places, so that they can be smoothly circulated. This seems to imply the intention of maintaining the circulation of domestic goods amid strict inspections. Therefore, we respectfully request your ministry to quickly order the national Customs to approve our request to facilitate transportation and sales and maintain domestic silk. We await your orders with utmost urgency. Sincerely, Jiangsu-Zhejiang Silk and Satin Weaving Federation.

The mainland newspaper reports that the British Labor Travel Association, whose purpose is to eliminate international discrimination, had twenty male and female representatives of the association arrive in Shanghai on the President Wilson on Sunday. The Labor Travel Association was formed at the International Labor Conference in Geneva after the end of the European War. He firmly believes that the closer the contact between people in the labor circles of various countries, the more it can eliminate wars and international misunderstandings. Therefore, after returning to his country at that time, he held this idea and established the Labor Travel Association. In the first year, a total of 700 people traveled to Europe. Last year, no less than 20,000 people in the British labor circles traveled to Europe organized by the association. The association also receives labor travelers from other countries to England. The group stayed in Shanghai for thirty-six hours and then took the original ship to South China.

The Real Estate Industry Cables the Ministry of Finance to Save the Right of Real Estate Sub-Mortgage, Which Is Greatly Related to the Entire Financial System. The Banking and Money Industries Are All Paying Great Attention to It.

The New Voice News Agency reports that the Shanghai Real Estate Industry Association, in order to save the real estate industry, with the support of the Banking and Money Industries Association, has telegraphed the Ministry of Finance to forward a request to the judiciary for an explanation of "if real estate A is mortgaged to B, and B then mortgages it to C, and B has gone bankrupt, then the real estate held by C is only an ordinary claim under the new law and cannot obtain a preferential claim" in order to save the situation. The original telegram will be released after Shen Tianxin, chairman of the association, returns to Shanghai from Wuhu. A reporter from the New Voice News Agency inquired from the banking and money industries yesterday that members of the banking and money industries consider the sub-mortgage of real estate to be a very common event. Since the First Special Zone Court cited the new law in the case of Chengyu Money Shop suing Dingzhen Money Shop, the real estate industry and the banking and money industries have been panicked because it is greatly related to the entire financial system. For example, banks and money shops have received a large number of sub-mortgaged real estate. If they cannot obtain priority rights and are regarded as ordinary claims, the risk is too great. At the same time, the Bank of China, Bank of Communications, and the Third Bank receive loan collateral from various banks and money shops, with real estate accounting for a large proportion. These real estate are all sub-mortgaged. Therefore, they hope that the judicial organs will remedy the situation.
