This is what my brother hopes from you all. Therefore, the saying that putting yourself in a deadly place will lead to survival is also the truth. Thank you for your love."

Nantong Water Police Passed Through Wusong Yesterday to Suppress Mutinying Soldiers of the Sijiao Security Corps 82

Sijiao, Shengshan, and other islands outside the Sanjiashuikou of Wusong have always been gathering places for fishermen, isolated overseas and plagued by pirates. A security corps was specially formed for self-defense. Previously, it was organized by Water Police Captain Xu Wen (also known as Wen Dounan, nephew of the First Bureau Chief Wen Zhaoyi) and was under the jurisdiction of Chongming County. Since the corps was formed, peace has prevailed. The First Brigade was stationed on Shengshan, and the Second Detachment was stationed on Sijiao, with a total of more than eighty soldiers. Because Xu was from Anhui, most of the soldiers were also from Anhui. After Xu Wen's death a few years ago, the influence of the Anhui faction declined. Xu's detachment leader on the island (also from Anhui) was replaced last month due to an incident and was succeeded by a certain Shen, who was from Chongming. After taking office, Shen dismissed many soldiers from Anhui on various pretexts. Those who were dismissed were stranded on the island, suffering from hunger and cold. Moreover, the corps had been in arrears with pay for several months, so the dismissed soldiers colluded with soldiers from Anhui who were still in service. On the evening of the 4th of this month, they went to the corps headquarters, seized firearms, and shot dead one soldier who refused to join them. They then marched to the district office, took District Chief Ling Diaocheng, who was already asleep, into custody, and demanded the surrender of 480 yuan in foreign currency. They then opened fire several times and escorted Ling to the beach, where they detained him on a pre-arranged sailboat. Afterwards, they went to Detachment Leader Shen's residence to report to the captain that the soldiers had mutinied. Upon hearing the report, the captain was about to go to the corps to investigate when gunfire suddenly erupted behind him, and Captain Shen was killed. The mutineering soldiers held a meeting on the beach of the island the next morning (the 5th), summoned local people, and announced Shen's crimes, such as using private connections and excluding dissidents, stating that they had been unable to bear it and had shot him. They then claimed that the corps was heavily in arrears with pay and needed to be allocated funds by the local authorities, ordering the first and second security groups of fishermen to each contribute 500 yuan. The first security group managed to raise 500 yuan and paid it, but the second security group was unable to raise funds, resulting in the abduction of ten fishermen, who were held on the sailboat. Among those kidnapped was Hu Yuansen, the island's richest man, who independently contributed 2,000 yuan to release all those who had been kidnapped. At that time, the mutineering soldiers, having achieved their goal, wanted to flee elsewhere. However, District Chief Ling was still on the boat, which was very inconvenient. They intended to release him, but they were afraid that after his release, he would send a telegram to request troops from other places to suppress them, which would be unfavorable. Therefore, they dragged District Chief Ling to the beach, fired a shot, and killed him. With a loud roar, they all went aboard the boat, sailed into the sea, and fled to other places. After the incident, an investigation revealed that a total of three people had been shot dead, 2,980 yuan in cash had been extorted, and one hundred and several dozen firearms belonging to the security corps and local civilian self-defense forces had been seized. Upon hearing the news, the Chongming County government telegraphed Zhu Aizhou, the chief of the Third District of the Nantong Water Police, requesting him to send troops to pursue and arrest the mutineers. After receiving the telegram, Chief Zhu ordered Special Task Force Captain Xu Zhaonan and Li Jianleng, the captain of the Second Squad stationed in Tong, to lead troops to Sijiao to investigate and suppress the mutineers. The squad passed through Wusong yesterday and is heading to Sijiao to investigate.

National Assembly Election Headquarters - Gray Telegram Clarification - One Person May Not Have Two Nomination Rights 84

Central News Agency reports: The Shanghai Municipal National Assembly Delegate Election Office received a gray telegram from the National Assembly Delegate Election Headquarters yesterday, clarifying that each person can only have one nominating right when nominating candidates. The original text reads: "To the Shanghai Election Supervisor: The nomination of National Assembly delegates is a type of delegate election. According to Article 5 of the National Assembly Delegate Election Law, each elector shall not have more than one electoral right. Therefore, a nominator should not be allowed to participate in more than two nominations. If a person has the qualifications of a nominator for more than two types of elections, they should follow the regulations regarding electors in Article 5 of the Election Law. In addition to informing separately, this is telegraphed for your information and distribution to all subordinates. National Assembly Delegate Election Headquarters, Gray You Tong." It is heard that the office has already forwarded the information. The reporter notes that the original text of Article 5 of the National Assembly Delegate Election Law reads: "Each elector shall not have more than two electoral rights. Those who have the right to vote in both regional and occupational elections shall participate in the occupational election. Those who have the right to vote in both special and occupational elections shall participate in the special election. Those who have more than two electoral rights in the occupational election shall choose to be an elector of one organization."

Zhejiang Government Bond Consolidation to be Printed Soon, Negotiating Exchange Methods with Silver Firms, Preparing to Establish Government Bond Fund Custody Committee 85

New Voice News: The 60 million yuan Zhejiang Province Government Bond Consolidation of the Republic of China Year 25, after its issuance on May 16th, the bonds were printed by the China Bookstore. The details are as follows: Consolidation of Public Debt

Exchange Method

The consolidation of public debt will be printed soon. Cheng Yuanfan, Director of the Zhejiang Finance Department, has negotiated with the silver firms on the exchange of the consolidation public debt and decided to adopt the unified public debt method. After the negotiation is completed, a public announcement will be made to entrust the Central Bank of China, Bank of Communications, and Zhejiang Local Bank, and the treasuries of each county to handle the exchange. The public debt is divided into four categories: the first category is 4.5 million yuan in bonds, with a term of 14 years and an annual interest rate of 8%; the second category is 17 million yuan in bonds, with a term of 16 years and an annual interest rate of 7%; the third category is 10.5 million yuan in bonds, with a term of 18 years and an annual interest rate of 6%; the fourth category is 28 million yuan in bonds, with a term of 22 years and an annual interest rate of 6%.

Establishment of Fund Association

The Zhejiang Provincial Government Bond Consolidation Fund Custody Committee has had each of the Ministry of Finance, the Audit Department, and the Zhejiang Finance Department each send a representative, the Bankers Association, the Money Dealers Association, and the Hangzhou Chamber of Commerce each recommend two representatives, and the creditors from Shanghai and Hangzhou elect three representatives to proceed with the organization. As for the use of the public debt, the first category will be used to repay old debts, public road bonds, and fixed-term loan vouchers; the second category will be used to repay construction public debt and disaster relief debt; the third category will be used to repay the cleaning up of old debts and treasury bills; and the fourth category will be used to repay local public debt and the mortgaged collateral of the original loans.

Supplementary Interest Payment

The principal and interest due on April 30th of (1) the 13th installment of the Construction Public Debt was re-drawn on July 13th, and from July 16th, in addition to the principal, the overdue interest from May 1st to July 15th was also paid. Those who were not drawn will be paid supplementary interest from May 1st to 15th. (2) 64% of the principal balance of the 9th installment of the Treasury Bills will be supplemented with interest from May 10th to 15th, and payments will be made from July 16th. The payment matters will be handled by the Central Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, the Agricultural and Industrial Bank of China, and other four banks.

Business Guidelines of Various Commercial Banks and Money Shops: Lending is Particularly Cautious 88

According to New Voice News, after the implementation of the new monetary system, although various industries have become active, they are still in decline due to the deep impact of the economic downturn. The business guidelines after this, in addition to stability, have to be changed. Although the commercial banks have had some surplus in the first half of the year, it is significantly less than in previous years. In addition, after the Central Trust Bureau and the China Bank of Communications established savings departments, deposits have increased sharply, so the savings deposits of commercial banks are inevitably affected. From the second half of the year, they have unanimously tightened up and are particularly cautious about various loans except for agriculture. Credit loans are reduced as much as possible. For example, the merger of the Jiangzhe and Zhonghui Banks, the closure of branches of the Zhongfu Silk Industry Bank, and the preparation for liquidation of the Guotai and Huaan Banks are all examples of this. In addition, various money shops are also particularly cautious about various loans due to the difficulty of business, especially credit loans, because the larger the loan, the greater the risk. For example, the suspension of listing of Hengyu and Hengji Exchange Money Shops and the suspension of new loans by Putai Deji Yuanzi Money Shop are all examples of this. However, the state banks, the Central Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, and the Agricultural Bank of China, etc., have expanded their business due to the implementation of the currency system policy, such as regulating interbank finance and assisting agriculture, industry, and commerce, all of which have had significant effects in practice.

It has begun on July 1. Regarding the pilot's license, the association has stipulated a renewal period. The public notice is recorded as follows: The provisional pilot certificates issued by the association earlier are now due for renewal for the 25th year (ie, from July 1, 1936, to June 30, 1937). The renewal period is specifically set from August 20th to September 30th of this year. Pilots holding temporary practice certificates must bring their own certificates and the fee of 15 yuan in national currency within the above-mentioned dates to the Songhan District Pilotage Office of the association for renewal. If it is really impossible to come in person, they must state the reasons why they cannot come in person in writing to the Songhan District Office, and transfer it to the port captain closest to the staff (ie, Hankou, Jiujiang, Wuhu, and Nanjing) for handling. The latest date for this renewal is September 30th, and no reissue will be made after the deadline without very special reasons. The old temporary practice certificates that have not been renewed will be invalid, and all parties must pay attention to this. The announcement is made to inform all relevant pilots to comply with this.

Buddhist Nun Disputes Temple Property 94

Buddhist nun Xiujing, also known as Juezheng, and her fellow nuns Zijian and Yuandao are in court over the temple property of Wannan Temple in Tanzi Bay, resulting in a major dispute. Xiujing filed a lawsuit in the District Court against Zijian and Yuandao, alleging that they occupied the temple property, colluded to embezzle it, and publicly insulted her. She claimed that in 1922, she came to Wannan Temple in Beitanzi Bay to practice devoutly. At that time, the abbot of the temple was the late Master Zhikong. In the autumn of 1925, the Master ordered the plaintiff to take over and ordered Zijian to take over as the abbot of Wanfu Temple on Taiyang Temple Road in Zhabei. However, in July 1931, Zhong Lin, a guest master living in the temple, took advantage of the plaintiff's absence to leave the temple for some reason and was instigated by the second defendant, Yuandao, to seize the temple. In November 1932, the plaintiff filed a lawsuit, and Zhong Lin lost the case. At that time, the second defendant saw that the situation was becoming increasingly dangerous and asked the old abbot of Huashan to mediate, instructing Zhong Lin to pay the plaintiff 1,000 yuan to sever ties with Zhong Lin. Chang Shi, a member of Baohua Mountain, appointed Zhong Lin as the manager of Wannan Temple and established a settlement agreement. On the second day of the fifth lunar month of this year, Zhong Lin died of illness, and the plaintiff brought a license from Huashan to Shanghai to take over, but unexpectedly, the first defendant colluded with the second defendant to seize the temple and coerced and publicly insulted her in every possible way. She reported to the police and was ordered to file a lawsuit according to law. The defendants committed the crimes of Article 335, Paragraph 1, and Article 309, Paragraph 1, of the Criminal Code. Zijian and Yuandao responded that the plaintiff was the first defendant's disciple, and the Wannan Temple and Wanfu Temple were both handed over to the first defendant by his master Zhikong. The second defendant was also the first defendant's eldest disciple, and the plaintiff was only an assistant to Wannan Temple. Therefore, the highest supervisory power still belonged to the first defendant, and he had fled since the Shanghai war and returned to Shanghai in 1932, when he was involved in a lawsuit with Zhong Lin and received 1,000 yuan, giving Wannan Temple to Zhong Lin and donating the deed to Baohua Mountain, which violated Buddhist laws and temple rules. Since he had already received the money and severed ties, he was not allowed to return to the temple. Wannan Temple was supervised and managed by the first defendant, and there were registration books from the Buddhist Association and the Public Security Bureau. He repeatedly intended to retake the temple, and the Buddhist Association and Wang Binyan and other gentlemen also opposed the plaintiff's takeover. As for the point of public insult, what evidence was there? He should be ordered to produce evidence, etc. Yesterday, Judge Wu Xiangzu opened the court for the hearing. The plaintiff withdrew the point of public insult in court. As for the embezzlement case, an order was given to summon the witnesses for further verification.

National Coal Mining Industry Joint Business Method Delimits Each District, Stipulates Production and Sales Limits, Delivers to Joint Affairs Preparatory Office for Proper Discussion 95

The National Coal Mining Industry Joint Office was decided to be established at the Mining Conference convened by the Ministry of Industry. After the preparatory committee members were nominated and a preparatory office was established in Shanghai, and two meetings were held, after drafting the organizational charter, it was sent to each mine to solicit opinions in order to submit it to the Second National Coal Mining Industry Representatives Conference to be held this weekend (15th) for discussion. During the session, the charter will be passed and the date of establishment will be determined and started. More than 30 major coal mines nationwide, currently more than 20 have reported to the meeting. The Ministry of Industry has telegraphed Director of the Mining Bureau Cheng Fayi to come to the meeting to guide. As for the joint business methods of the national coal industry, it was also discussed at the Mining Conference. At that time, two methods were proposed: one was to delineate each district in the country, and the coal mines in the district would produce and sell as much as possible locally; the other was to stipulate the production and sales limits of each mine according to the production and sales volume of each mine over the years. After detailed discussion, it was decided to deliver it to the preparatory office of the joint office for proper discussion. Therefore, the joint operation method will be discussed and decided upon in the long term after the establishment of the office.

Two Special District Court Presidents Wang Simo Referred for Disciplinary Action: Investigation Reveals Illegal Protectionism and Neglect of Duty in the Xiamen Commercial Bank Liquidation Case 97

Xinsheng News Agency reports that the Supervisory Yuan has announced that Wang Simo, President of the Shanghai Second Special District Court, and Judge Tu Shenjie engaged in illegal protectionism. The Supervisory Yuan has requested the Central Government Employees Disciplinary Committee to take disciplinary action. The relevant documents are recorded below:

Impeachment Document from the Supervisor

Supervisor Ding Chaowu's impeachment document states: Regarding the proposal for impeachment, the Secretariat of the Executive Yuan, in document No. 1178, forwarded a memorandum from Supervisory Committee members Hu Boyue, Bai Rui, Tian Jiongjin, and Cheng Yunpeng, stating that Ye Qinghua, the legal representative of the Xiamen Commercial Bank's Shanghai branch, had filed a complaint alleging illegal actions and abuse of power by Wang Simo, President of the Shanghai Second Special District Court. After review, it was recommended that the Secretariat issue a letter to the Jiangsu Supervisory District Supervisor's Office for investigation. The Executive Yuan approved this recommendation. Accordingly, the relevant documents, including original file No. Di Zi 868, are hereby forwarded for investigation and handling. Upon receipt, this office immediately dispatched Section Chief Huang Sen to conduct a thorough investigation. The following is a summary of the investigation report: (1) Regarding the collusion of Judge Tu Shenjie with associates: The plaintiff believes that the ruling of the Jiangsu Shanghai Second Special District Court on August 10, 1935, was procedurally flawed in two respects: A. Judge Tu Shenjie, based on the application of Yuanji Chen Yongyuan and others, immediately removed Sun Zhongyao as liquidator without requiring the petitioning shareholders to present their stock certificates or examining the reasons for the removal. However, according to Judge Tu's statement, after receiving the petition, the court summoned both parties for investigation. Sun Zhongyao was questioned about the shares listed in the petition of Yuanji and others. After reviewing the list, he acknowledged that there were no discrepancies. Therefore, following the usual practice of investigating evidence, since the facts were undisputed by the opposing party, there was no need to order the presentation of stock certificates. B. Although Tu Shenjie was aware that the petitioner had reached a settlement in the Shanghai First Special District Court, since the liquidator Sun Zhongyao had discovered that the company's assets were insufficient to cover its debts, he did not apply for bankruptcy as required by Article 23 of the Company Law, but instead sought a settlement with a small number of creditors. Therefore, even though it was a settlement during trial, the court could revoke it. (2) Regarding the overturning of the original ruling by the Third Branch of the Jiangsu High Court and the subsequent abuse of administrative power in detaining ships: The ruling of the Third Branch of the Jiangsu High Court was decided at 9:00 AM on September 27, 1935, and received on October 3. However, the draft letter from Wang Simo, in his capacity as president, to the Commissioner of Customs of the Jianghai Customs, was prepared on September 26... The following day, it was sent out. The claim that Wang Simo knew about the overturning of the Second Special District Court's ruling by the Third Branch is inconsistent with the facts. Furthermore, after the petitioner presented the fact that the ruling had been overturned and requested the revocation of the previous order, the response stated that it should wait for the file to be returned by the higher court for further review. However, after the Second Special District Court received the overturning of the original ruling from the Third Branch of the High Court, but before making a new ruling, the request to revoke the detention order was still not processed, indicating intentional obstruction, which is legally inappropriate. A. Regarding knowingly sending a letter to the Commissioner of Customs after the ruling had been overturned: The draft letter from Wang Simo, in his capacity as president, to the Commissioner of Customs of the Jianghai Customs, was prepared on September 26. The ruling overturning the decision by the higher court was decided on the 27th of the same month and received on October 3. Before the ruling was final, the court president's request to detain the four ships was not illegal under the law. B. The Second Special District Court sent a letter to the Commissioner of Customs of the Jianghai Customs based on the report of accountant Xu Yongzuo. However, the court never recognized the transfer of ownership of the Fu Dong, Fu Xi, and other ships, and continued to refer to them as belonging to the Fu Ning Commercial Shipping Company Limited. This difference in legal perspective should not be considered a disregard for the law or an intentional bias. C. Regarding acting beyond authority: The Commissioner of Customs of the Jianghai Customs is not the competent authority, and the court president's direct communication with them...

Dancer Fan Lingmei Leaves Datong and Joins Saint Anna: Accused of Breach of Contract, Datong Seeks Compensation of Over One Thousand Gold Pieces; Case Postponed for Reconciliation Possibility 98

Fan Lingmei, a Suzhou woman residing in Xiangkang Lane, Meibaige Road, is 21 years old. She used to work as a prostitute in the Liangmu brothel in the Little Garden. Due to the economic downturn in recent years, dance halls have flourished, greatly impacting the brothels. She had no choice but to seek alternative employment, using her daytime leisure time to work as a dancer in dance halls such as Yangtze, while continuing to work at night as before. In October of last year, Fan Lingmei transferred to Datong Dance Hall. Due to her beauty and skillful dancing, she was welcomed by the dance patrons. Fan Lingmei then left her life of selling laughter and began working as a dance partner. She signed a contract with Datong Dance Hall for a term of six months. Although the contract expired in April of this year, Datong, considering Fan to be a star of the hall, was reluctant to let her leave and continued the contract for another six months. Unexpectedly, in June of this year, Fan Lingmei had a disagreement with Datong Dance Hall and resolutely left to dance at Saint Anna Dance Hall. Datong Dance Hall believes that Fan Lingmei should not have rashly transferred elsewhere before the contract expired. According to the contract, if one party violates the contract, they must compensate the other party for the losses. Therefore, they retained lawyers Xu Shihao and Rong Ji to file a petition with the First Special Court for mediation. The mediation failed, and a formal lawsuit was filed, requesting the court to order Fan Lingmei to compensate for the losses of over 1,600 yuan. The case was heard yesterday morning at 8:20 AM in the Civil Tenth Court by Judge Xu Fuji. Lawyer Rong Jilong appeared on behalf of the plaintiff to state the case. The defendant Fan Lingmei did not appear, and the lawyer appeared and stated that there was hope for reconciliation in this case, so he requested a postponement. The court ruled that the case would be postponed to the 19th for another hearing. ...in procedures. To speed up matters, but not follow procedures, is not a valid reason. D. Appointing accountant Xu Yongzuo to perform accounting duties before the ruling was final: The First Special District Court's separate appointment of a liquidator based on the application of an interested party is in compliance with the provisions of Article 205, Paragraph 1 of the Company Law. E. Denying the validity of the liquidator's actions before the court formally removed him from office: Article 58 of the Company Law stipulates the duties of the liquidator and clearly states that the liquidator has the power to represent the company in all actions in the performance of the aforementioned duties. Before the court formally removed him from office, his actions were valid. However, after taking office as liquidator, Sun Zhongyao did not immediately apply for bankruptcy in accordance with Articles 214 and 63, Paragraph 1 of the Company Law when he discovered that the company's assets were insufficient to cover its debts. Instead, he entered into a settlement agreement with a portion of the creditors. The court believed that the liquidator had indeed violated his duties as a liquidator and therefore removed him from office on August of 1935, and simultaneously appointed accountant Xu Yongzuo as liquidator, which is legally appropriate. However, this accountant did not publish the notice until November 18, causing considerable damage to the rights of the creditors, which is not appropriate. This office has reviewed that the court's removal of Sun Jiayao as liquidator, the separate appointment of Xu Yongzuo as liquidator, and the detention of ships in this case are not inappropriate under the law. However, this detention order was based on Xu Yongzuo's application. The court did not follow procedures and hurriedly sent a letter to the non-competent Jianghai Customs Commissioner, and after receiving the higher court's overturning of this ruling, but before making a new ruling, the applicant requested the revocation of the detention order, and the court responded by stating that it should wait for the file to be returned by the higher court, delaying it for almost four months. When this office's staff arrived for investigation, it had not yet been processed, and the liquidator appointed by the court had also delayed the publication of the notice by more than three months beyond the statutory period, causing considerable losses to the creditors. The circumstances clearly indicate illegal protectionism, and it is appropriate to file an impeachment according to law. It is requested that the current President of the Shanghai Second Special District Court, Wang Simo, and the responsible judge, Xu Shenjie, be...

Leather Shoe Deliveryman Strangled to Death by Kidnappers: Two Robbers Sentenced to Death 99

Huang Futian, a 27-year-old man from Haimen and employee of the Gaohe Leather Shoe Store at 191 Tongfu Road, was instructed by his brother Fuzhao to deliver two pairs of leather shoes and one pair of women's shoes to a customer surnamed Yuan in room 529 of the Yangtze Hotel around 10:00 PM on May 16. When he proceeded to the Oriental Hotel room 324 to deliver shoes for a customer surnamed Wang, he was lured by robbers to the kitchen area of 15 Ma'an Lane, Chongqing Road. They used kidnapping methods to tie him up, causing him to call for help and leading to his death. Subsequently, they sent a letter to his brother Fuzhao demanding a ransom of 30,000 yuan, hoping to get lucky. Detectives Zhang Desheng, Hua Youshan, and Zhang Yaoji of the Hongkou Police Department apprehended the suspects, Liu Zongyou and Hu Shili, both from Ningbo, in Ninghai County and at 82 Kunming Road, Shanghai, along with the murder weapon. They were handed over to the First Special District Court for detailed interrogation. After deliberation, the court announced the sentence yesterday morning. Judge Xiao Xieffen presided over the Third Criminal Court and declared the following main points: Liu Zongyou and Hu Shili committed joint kidnapping for ransom and intentionally killed the victim. Each is sentenced to death and deprived of political rights for life. The small knife is confiscated. In addition to disciplinary action, the above measure is to maintain the rule of law. Respectfully submitted.

Committee Review Report

Supervisory Committee members Yu Hongqi, Wang Pingqi, and Liu E'qing stated in their review report: Regarding the review report, the Jiangsu Supervisor Ding Chaowu impeached Wang Simo, President of the Shanghai Second Special District Court, for illegal protectionism. The committee members jointly reviewed the case and concluded that in handling the debt dispute between the Xiamen Commercial Bank's Shanghai branch and the Shanghai Fu Ning Commercial Shipping Company Limited, the court, regarding the ships transferred to the creditor group, the Xiamen Commercial Bank's Shanghai branch, issued a detention order without following procedures and hurriedly sent a letter in the name of the President of the Shanghai Second Special District Court to the non-competent Jianghai Customs Commissioner. After receiving the higher court's overturning of this ruling, but before making a new ruling, the transferee requested the revocation of the detention order, but the court delayed the matter for more than three months, failing to process it. This constitutes illegal protectionism. Furthermore, the liquidator appointed by the court delayed the public announcement by three months beyond the statutory period, causing unwarranted damage to the creditors. This is also a neglect of duty. The impeached persons are indeed guilty of illegal protectionism and neglect of duty. It is requested that Wang Simo, President of the Shanghai Special District Court, and Tu Shenjie, the responsible judge, be referred for disciplinary action. Respectfully submitted.

Headless Female Corpse Discovered in Front of the Rowing Club: Wicker Suitcase Not Luggage, Suspicion Raised by Western Police 102

Yesterday afternoon around 8:20, a Western police officer patrolling Suzhou Road in the Public Concession discovered a flat, wicker suitcase in front of the Shanghai Westerner Rowing Club. Initially, he thought it was luggage piled up by the club, so he didn't pay attention. However, after noticing that no one had claimed it for a long time, he became suspicious and went forward to inspect it. To his shock, the basket contained nothing else but the corpse of a woman around 20 years of age. The head was missing, and the limbs had been cut into four pieces, along with one piece of the body. It was a bloody and gruesome sight. Upon seeing this, the Western police officer immediately reported it to the police station, which dispatched detectives to investigate. They concluded that it was a case of murder and the body had been dumped there. The corpse was transferred to the coroner's office for examination. The identity of the deceased and the reason for her murder are still under close investigation.

Singing Girl Wu Peilan Accuses Song Gengsheng: Affection Grows During Banquets, Cohabitation and Childbirth, Then Abandonment 108

Wu Rongsheng, a 51-year-old man from Suzhou, resides at No. 1 Menpai, Sanxin Lane, Ailege Road, Beichujiaqiao, French Concession. He has a daughter named Peilan, who is 20 years old this year. She studied drama in her childhood and performed at the Qunfanghui in the Great World. Every day at dusk, she also sang at various restaurants and taverns. Because of her good looks and artistic skills, the family of father and daughter was still able to make a living. Two years ago, when Peilan was singing at the Quanxingkang Hotel north of Xianshi Company on Zhejiang Road, Song Gengsheng (38 years old this year) from Hubei, who lived at No. 9 Chongan Lane, Haifang Road, happened to be drinking with friends. He met Peilan and asked her to perform. During the entertainment, Wu and Peilan exchanged glances. After the banquet, they went to the Great Shanghai Hotel and lingered there. Since then, the two developed a relationship. Later, the two decided to meet every Saturday night. Until last year, Peilan had a child named Xiaomaotou. Since then, Song Gengsheng's traces of contact with Peilan have gradually become estranged. Now, Wu Rongsheng, Peilan's father, in his capacity as legal guardian, along with his daughter Peilan, retained a lawyer to file a special lawsuit in the criminal court of the Second Special Court, accusing Song Gengsheng of harming the family. The court accepted the lawsuit. Yesterday morning, Criminal Court President Wang Gangxu presided over the Second Criminal Court to summon them for questioning. First, the plaintiffs, father and daughter, described the course of the case, and then the lawyer hired by the defendant to defend him, Mr. Xu Xuzhang, arrived in court to await questioning and filed a counterclaim for false accusation. According to the defendant Song Gengsheng, what the plaintiff said was not true. He claimed that two years ago, when the defendant was socializing with friends at the Quanxingkang Hotel, a singer named Wu Shunbao, i.e., Peilan, came forward to solicit singing. He got to know her by soliciting songs. Later, the woman recommended herself and learned that in addition to singing, she also worked as a prostitute. The defendant was negligent for a while and had a physical relationship with her, but each time he paid a night fee of five or six yuan. Her father and mother both knew about it. Wu Shunbao is still in the singing industry and sings in the Qunfanghui in the Great World. Her parents regard her as a cash cow and monitor her closely, never leaving her side. Her whole family lives in Sanxin Lane, and everyone knows about it, and Li Jianxian can testify to this. As for cohabitation and childbirth with the defendant, it is all fictitious. It is appropriate to punish the counterclaim for false accusation, etc. After verifying the confessions in court, it was announced that the hearing would be postponed to another date.

When the association's undertakings are related to various members or fellow provincials, they may provide a corresponding guarantee. Have complete eligibility to be elected (Note) For officers such as members of the Fund Management Committee, whose term of office is more than one year, only permanent basic members may be elected. B. When members need to be subsidized for weddings, funerals, or special events, the association may notify them. C. Other rights and interests that belong to the association's scope of duties and are not specified in the articles of association may also be enjoyed by special instructors, special sponsors, or special board members and special members in Shanghai. Pan Xulun and Others Initiate the Establishment of a United Insurance Adjusting Office 112

With the aim of ensuring insurance premiums are not wasted, prominent Shanghai accountants Pan Xulun, Yu Haifan, and others, in light of the increasing development of insurance services and the growing number of loss compensation cases, and due to the lack of research on insurance matters by Chinese citizens, which leads to frequent disputes, have established the United Insurance Adjusting Office. The aim is to seek fair and appropriate resolutions in the event of loss compensation disputes between insurance companies and policyholders. The following is a record of its origins: Regarding the establishment, our accountants have observed that domestic fire and marine insurance services are increasingly developing, and loss compensation cases are becoming more frequent. However, among Chinese individuals, there are few who specialize in notarization and serve insurance companies and policyholders. Therefore, we have gathered experts from various industries to establish the United Insurance Adjusting Office, which has been approved by the Ministry of Industry and Commerce for registration to perform the duties of a notary public. We aim to thoroughly reform existing malpractices and maintain a fair and impartial attitude to seek a fair and appropriate resolution for both insurance companies and policyholders in the event of loss compensation. Since commencing practice, we have accumulated practical experience and deeply feel that Chinese citizens still lack sophisticated research into insurance matters. This is because they are unclear about insurance regulations, or neglect prior planning, or during the effective period of the contract, do not understand the conditions that must be observed, or after an accident, do not know the appropriate steps to take. As a result, they waste excessive premiums, increase unnecessary burdens, and when they suffer losses, they cannot obtain appropriate compensation, leading to severe and irreparable damage, which is a common occurrence. The pain of not being able to obtain adequate compensation after suffering a loss is well understood by those who have experienced an accident or are familiar with the situation. The waste of premiums at ordinary times, though limited in each instance, accumulates into a large sum over time. This kind of intangible loss should not be overlooked. The sole aim of insurance is originally to spend a small amount of premium in advance to prevent major disasters. Therefore, the payment of premiums should be based on the most economical principle, and the compensation after an accident should aim to make up for the entire loss. If both cannot be achieved, then the effectiveness of insurance is lost. However, this is not because the insurance system is not perfect, nor is it the original intention of insurance companies, but because policyholders do not seek professional insurance advice and fail to handle matters appropriately, leading to this outcome. Now, our accountants, with the original intention of serving society, seek to relieve all sectors from the above pain and waste, and have added the method of permanent insurance consultants to provide timely consultation for those who need insurance, entrusting them to plan so that premiums are not wasted, and in the future, in the event of an accident, they will not suffer significant losses even with insurance.

Former President of the District Court, Shen Xiqing, Passes Away 115

Shen Xiqing, former president of the Shanghai District Court, served in the legal profession for many years. After graduating from Waseda University in Japan at the end of the Qing Dynasty, he returned to China and served as a teacher at various law schools in Zhejiang. After the founding of the Republic, he successively served as a judge of the Zhejiang Provincial Court, a presiding judge of the higher courts of Zhejiang, Hunan, and Jiangsu, and the president of the Yongjia, Wuxian, and Shanghai district courts, as well as the president of the Shanghai District Court and the chairman of the Shanghai Municipal Civil Servants Disciplinary Committee. He was upright, enforced the law impartially, and eliminated accumulated abuses, earning a reputation wherever he went. For example, in Yongjia, he rebuilt the court building; in Changhu, he built staff dormitories; and in Changhu Court, he rebuilt the detention center, either by using surplus funds or by diligently managing with minimal funds, working hard and tirelessly to achieve success. In the sixteenth year, he also assisted in the recovery of the Mixed Court and made significant contributions. After resigning last summer, he suffered from hemorrhoids that were not healed after surgery, and then contracted a lung disease. He died in his hometown of Shaoxing on June 28. He served in the legal profession for nearly 30 years, maintaining integrity and living a simple life. After his death, he was impoverished, and those who heard of it felt sorry for him. His wife and daughters are now burying him in Baiyutan in his hometown, and many of his friends are attending the funeral. Alas, this honest official will forever rest in a mound of yellow earth among the mountains and waters of Kuaiji.

Continued Trial of the Tongyi Company Lawsuit - Another Creditor Joins the Lawsuit - 700,000 in Government Bonds Sold for 520,000 - Huang Suchu and Seven Others Absent, Trial Concluded Yesterday 116

Following the bankruptcy of the Tongyi Trust Company, its general manager Huang Suchu and all directors, supervisors, and assistant managers were successively sued for criminal self-accusation of fraud and embezzlement by Li Songtao and others who had deposited government bonds. The First Special District Court has investigated the circumstances, as reported previously. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Zhong Qing continued the investigation. The defendants Huang Suchu, Liu Fangyuan, Sun Xinzhong, Liu Renzan, Xiong Mulian, Wu Jing, and Chen Gongqia remained absent. Jiang Liuzhi was ill in the hospital, and Zhou Shouliang was dispatched to Guangdong by order of the Ministry of Finance, so he was also unable to attend in person.

The remaining Xu Jiyin, Guo Chushang, Chuan Zhuyin, Jin Weiqin, Deng Dongming, and Zhou Longzhan all attended the court with their defense lawyers. Liu Zikang, who was in custody, was also brought to the court. In addition to the original plaintiffs, Chen Yanying was newly added as a plaintiff. Chen stated the facts of the lawsuit, saying that 700,000 in 96 government bonds were deposited with the company. Later, due to a need for funds, she used the bonds to borrow 30,000 yuan. Subsequently, Jin Weiqin informed her that a portion of the bonds had been sold by the company. Now, after investigation by her lawyer, it has been found that 570,000 was sold.

Only 130,000 remains, etc. When questioned, Jin Weiqin stated that Chen pledged the deposited funds, and after Chen and Sun Xinzhong contacted each other, she learned that the company had sold a portion of them, so she notified Chen. She did not initially know how much was sold, etc. Xu Jiyin and Guo Yuchu both stated that they were not executive directors, so they were not clear about the company's business situation, and they did not know that the company's capital had been亏蚀 to the point of declaring bankruptcy, so it was difficult to make any claims, etc. Chuan Zhuyin also stated that he

was not originally a shareholder.

Only because he and Huang Suchu were from the same hometown, Huang came to invite him to be a supervisor the year before last winter, and sent him 1,000 yuan in stock, valued at 600 yuan. But although he served as a supervisor, he never attended meetings. He was not aware of the disposal of government bonds, etc. The court then ruled that the proceedings against Huang Suchu and the other seven defendants who had avoided court should be suspended, and the remaining persons should immediately begin their defense. Subsequently, the lawyers for the plaintiffs, Zhang Yifan, Le Junwei, Shi Ying, and others, jointly stated that the defendants had violated the criminal law by committing

fraud and embezzlement

and the reasons for violating the provisions of the Company Law, requesting that the responsible defendants be punished according to the law and demanding that the related civil suits be adjudicated together. Judge Zhong ruled that the related civil suits of the individual plaintiffs should be resolved together, and instructed the lawyers for the defendants to defend the defendants. First, lawyer Xu Shihao defended the Xu Ji and Zhou Shouliang's not being responsible for this case. The reasons are as follows: Xu and Zhou have been prosecuted in several cases because the company ceased operations. However, regarding criminal cases, one case has already ruled Xu and Zhou innocent. Regarding civil cases, a case was opened this morning, and the plaintiff in that case voluntarily withdrew the charges against Xu, Zhou, and other defendants. As for the charges of fraud and embezzlement brought by the plaintiffs in this case, they are all speculations about Xu and Zhou. After all, there is no evidence to prove whether Xu and Zhou committed fraud or privately mortgaged government bonds. How can one be placed in the law based on speculative evidence? Xu and Zhou have also repeatedly admitted that they did not know the capital

had already been depleted and the assets were insufficient to repay the debts. Of course, it was impossible to propose convening a meeting to declare bankruptcy. Moreover, the company's articles of association stipulate that the executive directors are responsible for executive affairs. Xu and Zhou are not executive directors. Of course, they do not know the company's situation and should be declared innocent and the related civil suit dismissed. It was decided that Guo Yuchang's lawyer would defend. Guo's position is equal to that of Xu and Zhou, so the reasons for the defense are also the same. Lawyer Shan Zaiyou defended Jiang Liuzhi, saying that Jiang

was previously a supervisor

but had not participated in company affairs for six or seven years and was not responsible for criminal liability. The Company Law cited by the plaintiffs mostly applies to directors and has nothing to do with supervisors. The lawyer for Chuan Zhuyin also said that although Chuan was a supervisor, he had never inquired about company affairs. In addition, the defense lawyers for Jin Weiqin, Deng Dongming, Zhou Longzhan, and Liu Zikang all defended their clients, saying that they were either unaware of the situation or served as general managers. After the defense, Judge Zhong ruled that the debate was concluded and the sentence would be pronounced on the afternoon of the 18th. Jin Weiqin and Zhou Longzhan each paid a bail of 2,000 yuan, and Liu Zikang was remanded in custody. After the ruling, the court adjourned at five o'clock.

Recently, in order to facilitate the local agricultural and commercial sectors, Minhang has been selected as a place where land and water transportation is smooth and local agricultural products are sold. A branch office has been specially set up, and a house has been rented on Minhang Street. Mr. Li Guangyuan, director of the Beiqiao branch of the bank, is responsible for actively planning and arranging everything. The decoration project can be completed this month, and the official opening is scheduled for the beginning of September. An agricultural warehouse will be set up along the Huangpu River in the town and will open at the same time to handle a large number of agricultural product storage operations.

The China International Famine Relief Commission Ends Jianghe Flood Disaster Donations 125

The China International Famine Relief Commission, located at 505 Henan Road, is a charitable organization registered with the Ministry of Interior. It usually devotes itself to construction to prevent natural disasters. In the event of a disaster, it will consider the situation and hold emergency relief work to seek relief. Over the past fifteen years, the water conservancy, transportation and cooperative undertakings it has handled have spread throughout the country, and the results have been very good. Last summer, the Yangtze River and Yellow River successively flooded, and disasters spread to several provinces. The association submitted a request to the Ministry of Interior to carry out Jianghe flood relief work, and strived to provide relief. All the work carried out was in accordance with the principles of being practical and swift, and efforts were made to carry it out. The survivors have been rescued and a large number of people have been saved. Recently, because the disaster situation in various places has gradually eased, and the urgent and work relief efforts have been completed one after another, there is no need to continue raising donations for the Jianghe flood disaster, and the collection of donations was terminated at the end of last month. In the future, it is planned to resume normal work and engage in construction. The donations collected this month will be used for construction projects.

Unused Revenue Stamps Should Not Be Stamped Separately 126

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce previously received a letter from Qiantaixiang Hardware Store, proposing to add a small red chop to the revenue stamps purchased and stored before they are used, and requested the Ministry of Finance to verify and instruct them. Now, the Ministry of Finance has approved and opened the mill's proxy telegram, and has learned that the revenue stamp is a national tax collection certificate. According to the provisions of Article 12 of the Stamp Duty Law, stamping or drawing a pledge at the riding seam between the tax ticket and the original paper surface is a cancellation symbol. If there are other stamps on the tax ticket, which are mixed with the cancellation symbol, and the distinction is not clear, it is easy to involve suspicion of reuse. Therefore, merchants should not affix another stamp to cause disputes, except for stamping the riding seam for cancellation after affixing the stamp. As for the special tax tickets for customs and other special purposes, all are stamped by the Ministry, and when merchants stamp them for cancellation, which is the cancellation stamp and which is the special stamp is obvious and different from the above situation. It is not convenient to cite it as an example. You should immediately transfer the instructions for notification in this batch.

Municipal Public Security Bureau Looking for Unnamed Boy 127

The Municipal Public Security Bureau reported that on the afternoon of August 9, at 2:00 PM, Song Houtian, a police officer from the Ximen Branch, found a lost unnamed boy in the Public Education Hall. He was three or four years old, with a round face and a monk's head, wearing a white cloth shirt, black cloth pants, pink socks, and white and red checkered shoes. The Statement That the Deadline for Licenses for the Transportation and Sale of Local Goods Is Approaching Is Not Accurate 128

Xin Sheng News Agency said that the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce's Private Inspection Committee announced that the newspaper reported yesterday that the deadline for licenses for the transportation and sale of local goods is approaching soon. The fact is not accurate. Although the Ministry of Finance previously stipulated that manufacturers of foreign goods who are engaged in inspection should register with the customs and obtain a license, with a limit of 20 days from the date of local promulgation, this is a deadline in terms of procedure. In fact, those who register with the customs and obtain a license recently, the customs is still continuing to process. As for the method of obtaining licenses for the transportation and sale of local goods, although the procedures are roughly the same as those for obtaining licenses for the transportation and sale of foreign goods, according to the customs announcement on July 27, there is no deadline.

Fire Department Ambulance Team: Affairs Becoming Increasingly Developed, Highest Record Set Last Month 130

The Public Concession Fire Department Chief's report for July indicated that the department received 56 fire alarms during the month, of which eight were false alarms. The property loss due to fires within the Public Concession was valued at 22,179 yuan, while in the Special Tax District, it was only 106 yuan. The value of property at risk of fire was over 7,996,000 yuan in the Public Concession and over 26,000 yuan in the Special Tax District. Furthermore, the department's ambulance team received 685 requests for assistance during the month, and 693 injured or sick individuals were transported to various hospitals by the team's ambulances. According to the team personnel, the number of requests received that month was the highest record since the team's establishment in January 1931.

Yangtze River Downstream Voyage: Customs Develops Speed Chart, Placing Parallel Ruler on Speed Line Allows Knowing When to Arrive at a Port 131

To facilitate merchants in easily calculating the voyage along the downstream Yangtze River, the Customs has specially printed a voyage speed chart, instructing various shipping companies to distribute it for use on Jianglun ships traveling between Shanghai and Hankou. The usage of the chart is explained as follows: "To use the voyage speed chart, place a parallel ruler on the estimated speed line of the ship and move it to the departure time, then you will know when you can arrive at a certain port."

Letter 134

To the Editor: This correspondent notes that various newspapers in Shanghai have reprinted a news item from Dagongbao entitled "Ministry of Finance Thoroughly Clears Private Goods and Establishes Shanghai Intelligence Office," which is largely inconsistent with the facts. While this office has been established, it is entirely of a trial nature and has only been approved by Minister Kong upon presentation by Li Weiqing personally to trial intelligence matters regarding investigating smuggling, bearing exclusive responsibility for intelligence, without executing tasks. There is no concrete organization internally. The thirty individuals comprising the intelligence unit are divided into three teams, and they notify anti-smuggling agencies and relevant military police based on what they have investigated. The communication office set up on Father Lao Road in the French Concession is also not an officially established agency, and that communication office has been moved to the Chinese area. The correspondent hereby informs and requests that you verify and correct this matter. Sincerely, Li Weiqing, August 11.

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that Shandong, the upper and middle reaches of the Yellow River, and the upper and middle reaches of the Yangtze River were mostly clear with thunderstorms and variable winds. Shen Bao National Products Special Issue

Contributions

Commending Restaurants that Use National Product Beverages 136

— Yang An

Once, while having dinner with some friends, one of them asked, "Why do waiters in restaurants always seem to prefer offering foreign beer and foreign soda to guests? What's the reason for this?" The answers at the time varied: (1) They're greedy for small profits. (2) They lack knowledge and don't understand the principles of patriotism. (3) They're following the owner's orders and willingly allowing rights to flow out. Such waiters, lacking a national perspective, are certainly unforgivable. However, the lack of enforcement power in society and the lack of a sense of right and wrong are also major reasons. I remember Mr. Chu Fucheng once loudly advocating at a meeting that there should be a cleansing movement in the food and beverage industry. What to cleanse? It's not selling foreign beer, not drinking foreign soda, from the errand boy to the waiter, to the shop assistant, manager, shareholder, and customer, everyone must have this mindset, everyone must hold this intention, and then the national products business will have hope for development.

Therefore, Hu Jun Xiyuan suggests that instead of passively punishing, it's better to actively encourage. Starting today, a legitimate national products organization should investigate whether a certain restaurant uses national product beer, soda, and all other consumables. Then, based on the investigator's accurate report, if it can be said that the restaurant absolutely does not use any foreign beverages, the national products organization or institution should give it a prominent plaque saying "Practicing National Product Beverages" or display the words "Completely National Products" so that customers can know at a glance. Doing this would be very effective. Otherwise, advising people or lecturing waiters will always be piecemeal and not very effective.

Smuggling Inspection and Promoting National Products 137

— Xuan Wan

Smuggling inspection and promoting national products are originally the only ways to save the national economy and revive industry and commerce. Therefore, these two aspects cannot be separated when discussing them. We know that smuggling inspection is a necessary task to protect domestic products, and expanding and strengthening the national product movement is the fundamental condition to eliminate smuggling.

Recently, regarding the future of smuggling inspection and promoting national products, we heard good news, which is that at the recent joint conference of chambers of commerce from various provinces and cities in Shanghai, they passed a proposal to organize the "General Association of Smuggling Inspection of Chambers of Commerce in Various Regions of the Republic of China." The establishment of this large-scale, voluntary smuggling inspection organization by the people comes at a time when the smuggling problem remains serious, especially when domestic industries suffer greatly and their situation becomes increasingly difficult. Its significance is very great, and its mission is even more important. We sincerely hope that it can have great success in suppressing smuggling and strictly preventing profiteers, and that it will make considerable efforts to develop domestic products and promote industry, fulfilling its duty to revive industry and commerce and promote the national economy.

We know that the thorough solution of the smuggling problem requires the voluntary rise of all the people of the country, which is very important. Because only when the general public understands that smuggled goods must not be bought or sold, regarding them as floodwaters and fierce beasts, then, even if smuggled goods can seep into all parts of the Chinese interior like mercury, they will never have the chance to change their appearance and be sold publicly again after being strictly prevented and mutually supervised by various chambers of commerce and other public organizations. Being unable to promote and sell them is the best way to fundamentally eliminate the smuggling problem. Finally, I would also like to earnestly hope that in the future, we must not only strive to investigate smuggling but also strive to promote the sales of national products, so that the development of national industries and smuggling inspection can be integrated into one, opening a bright path for the future national economic construction, and only by working hard in this way can we better satisfy the ardent expectations of the people of the country.

National Economic Construction Movement and Promoting National Products 138

— Pan Yangyao

Promoting national products is a matter of life and death for China today, and the urgency is very different from what it was one or two decades ago. Just ask, the customs revenue is over tens of millions of yuan annually, and tax evasion and smuggling are also over one or two tens of millions of yuan. The outflow of huge amounts of silver every year is even more uncompensated. How much wealth do the people have? How can they not go bankrupt? If this continues without a solution, the national economy will be completely beyond repair in two or five years for a shorter period, or ten years for a longer period. Where would there be a place for national products? Therefore, promoting national products and using national products today is a work of saving the national economy, a work of seeking survival and saving life. It can be said to be the most important work of the country today. If one does not think that promoting national products is important, it is better to seek oneself than to seek others, it is better to save oneself than to beg for help, especially needing everyone to have a sense of public spirit, to be able to be self-aware, and to eliminate the ideas of the small self, to extinguish the thoughts of selfishness, and to unanimously dedicate their abilities and contribute to the national economy, to make strict protection, to avoid the attack of foreign goods. In my personal opinion, Chinese people today should have four ways of working hard for national products from the standpoint of the national economy.

(1) Unite the Strength of the Same Industry. The most important work for the survival of national product industries is the unity of the same industry. Therefore, uniting the strength of the same industry is essential for the self-rescue of the national products sector. Since ancient times, the biggest fatal wound in the failure of national products has not been external enemies but internal enemies, not foreign merchants but the same industry. Obviously, an industry with great promise, after many difficult creations or hard inventions, before long everyone imitates and emulates, without asking whether the supply and demand are corresponding, whether the needs are increasing, confused by the great profits, competing in groups, producing crudely and poorly, and lowering prices with each other. As a result, they feel the same difficulties and perish together, ultimately causing a certain industry to be completely wiped out, giving foreign goods a chance to sell well. Thinking about it afterward, it is truly heartbreaking. Therefore, today's cooperation between the same industry is a way for each individual to save themselves. Each person should join the same industry association, respect the regulations and resolutions of the same industry association, and go further to seek cooperation in the purchase of raw materials, cooperation in the sale of products, and in all aspects of production, the same industry should give full play to their strengths everywhere, for the development of the division of labor, in order to achieve effective cooperation, and the life of national products may be maintained or not abolished.

(2) Pay Attention to Improving Products. Our national products have indeed made progress compared to the past, but there are still many that are not satisfactory. Are the machinery and equipment excellent? Is the factory management proper? Is the personnel aspect comprehensive? Have all products reached the goal of standardization? Are the goods sold overseas welcomed by people? Those engaged in the national products business should always have a spirit of innovation, constantly research, and constantly improve, so that the quality of products can surpass others, and the future of national products will naturally feel bright.

(3) Find Ways to Reduce Costs. If we think that today the self-rescue of the national products sector means that the same industry should only help each other and save each other, and not kill each other in competition, then all competitive power between individuals does not lie in the promotion of value, but in the quality and cost. If we can strive to reduce costs in terms of cost and strive to make products exquisite in terms of production, we can be sure of victory, take the upper hand, and not worry about losses or failures. Therefore, today's national products sector should implement scientific management, conduct cost accounting, eliminate unnecessary waste, and eliminate unnecessary equipment and personnel, so that it can compete with the dumping of foreign goods.

(4) Study Buyer Psychology. A major problem with our national products is closing the door to build a car and sticking to one's own opinions without catering to the psychology of general users, so that all products are sold in area A but cannot be sold in area B. Selling products at the factory becomes easy to accumulate and stagnate, and capital is stagnant and turnover is poor, which is also a shortcoming of today's national products sector. If we can make the manufacturers study buyer psychology, focus on the preferences of users in various places, and strive for the modernization and simplification of products in order to promote the production of products as much as possible, then the difficulties of the past may be reduced.

The above refers to the manufacturers themselves. At the same time, sellers should also adhere to the idea of only selling national products, strive to promote sales, and do their best to serve, so that national products that have come from struggle and hard work have the opportunity to develop and promote. This is the most effective way to help the national economy. Furthermore, in terms of the government, the government does not need to say more, but to follow the essential methods: (1) improve the organization of the same industry and use gradual control, (2) reduce donations and taxes, abolish unreasonable special donations and special taxes in various provinces, (3) improve the transportation organization and reduce its costs at the same time, (4) join with the financial sector to organize an industrial loan syndicate as a backing for the national products industry and provide security for the financial sector, (5) lead the provinces, cities, and counties to connect the transportation and sales of machine products and local products so that machine products are transported internally and local products are sold externally, not only achieving the goal of barter but also inducing the purchasing power of inland rural areas and expanding the field of local products and national products, (6) assist rural sideline occupations in various places to enrich the lives of farmers, so that everyone has the ability to purchase national products, which is a basic work to promote national products.

At the same time, I also have advice for the general public: national products have today's achievements, and I don't know how much brainpower, how much effort, and how much blood and tears have been spent to get such a price. If national products are equal to foreign goods, use national products. If national products have the same value as foreign goods, use national products. Even if the quality of national products is inferior to foreign goods, use national products. If the value of national products is more expensive than foreign goods, use national products. National products should be forgiven everywhere, applied with guidance, supported, and determined. It is right and proper for Chinese people to use Chinese goods, there is nothing to doubt, there is nothing to consider. The Japanese who live in China use their own national products for everything, even a cigarette, a match, a piece of paper, a drink, a needle, and a thread. If they use foreign goods, they consider it a great disrespect and a lifelong shame. Is there any nation in the world that takes pride in using foreign goods? I love fashionable people who are happy to use foreign goods. Why not think about it, why not be self-aware? This alone is the way out for the national economy, in factories, in businesses, in the government, and in the people, and all can do it. If this is not done, it is equivalent to sitting and waiting for the country to perish, there is no excuse for it, and there is no escaping responsibility.

National products are especially vibrant in summer! As the fiery canopy hangs high, the heat is steaming people! If one returns home from public duties, barefoot, waving a cattail fan, living in a small home, and facing national products, how happy! Everything, national products in summer, are especially vibrant! Moreover, snow lotus root is used to mix ice, and plums and watermelons float! Short Message

The purpose of Meixing toothpaste is to develop abroad, so it is not very common in the market. It has a long and commendable history, which is worth mentioning. Three or four years ago, the South Seas Islands was the most popular time for Meixing toothpaste because of its pure quality and low price, which was welcomed by the local officials. But this also aroused great jealousy from foreign merchants, who used their special power to devise various methods to sabotage and encroach. A Dispute Arose in the Soccer Match: Peru Withdrew from the Conference: Unwilling to Hold a Rematch Against Austria: The Conference Cancelled the Peruvian Team's Qualifications: Left Berlin Today to Express Protest 142

(Berlin) The soccer teams of Peru and Austria held a match on the 8th of this month. As a result, Peru won with a score of four to two. Afterward, the Austrian team raised protests regarding the match situation and the audience's attitude. The conference authorities investigated the matter and decided to cancel the score and order both sides to replay the match yesterday afternoon. At that time, the Peruvian team did not appear. The referee then ruled that Austria won. All the Peruvian athletes were very dissatisfied with this matter and have now withdrawn from the conference to protest. (Havas, 11th dispatch)

Residents of the Capital Angered

(Reuters, Lima, Peru, 10th) Today, General Pina Videz ordered the Peruvian delegation to withdraw from the Berlin World Games to protest the cancellation of Peru's victory over Austria in soccer. The reason for the cancellation of Peru's victory was that some Peruvian supporters invaded the field during the match and attacked Austrian athletes. After being angered by the decision of the International Football Association, the residents of Lima gathered for a street meeting, and newspapers issued extra editions, declaring that all South American countries should withdraw from the conference to show solidarity with Peru.

Austria Gets the Right to Rematch

(National Shipping News Agency, Berlin, August 10) After Austria protested yesterday against the 4-2 defeat to Peru after extra time in the soccer match with Peru, the authorities announced today that the two countries' soccer teams will play again this afternoon. However, the Peruvian team is unwilling to play again, so Austria enjoys the right of the opponent to abstain and enter the semi-final week.

Peruvian Athletes Leave Berlin

(National Shipping News Agency, Berlin, August 10) The dispute between the Peruvian soccer team and the Austrian team has been reported in previous newspapers. Now, because the authorities did not accept the Peruvian side's opinion and reconsider the matter, all the Peruvian athletes attending the World Games decided to withdraw from the conference. It is heard that this decision was suggested by the Peruvian Embassy. It is heard that the athletes will leave Berlin tomorrow.

Deciding the Third Place Today

(Berlin, broadcast on the 11th) Yesterday's Italy vs. Norway soccer match was the quarter-final of the soccer championship of the conference. In the first half, Italy won against Norway with a score of 1-0. In the second half, Norway returned one goal, resulting in a 1-1 tie. After an extension of thirty minutes, Italy scored a goal in the first fifteen minutes. As a result, Italy won the final. The soccer skills of both sides were balanced and quite exciting. Today is the quarter-final of Austria vs. Poland. The winner will decide the final with Italy on the 15th, and the loser will compete with Norway for third and fourth place on the 13th.

Germany Said Not Responsible

(National Shipping News Agency, Berlin, August 11) Regarding FIFA's acceptance of Austria's protest, Baron Latour, Chairman of the International Olympic Committee, gave a statement to the press this morning, saying that this decision was completely based on technical issues. The International Olympic Committee and the World Games Organizing Committee have nothing to do with this matter. These two organizations also have no right to question the FIFA decision. Therefore, the German Sports Authority has absolutely no responsibility to bear for this matter. Germany also has no representative participating in the FIFA Arbitration Committee.

Berlin, August 10th, via Reuters. Chinese heavyweight boxing athlete Wang Runlan was eliminated by Fouk of the Netherlands in the first week of competition in a swift match today. Fouk had more experience, throwing punches from both left and right, fiercely attacking Wang’s body. Although Wang’s upper lip was broken in the third round, he continued to fight to the end.

Berlin, August 10th, via the Allied News Agency. The boxing preliminary rounds started at the Games today. Nakano of Japan fought against Savolainen of Finland. Nakano consistently attacked with left jabs and right straight punches. However, when the time was up, the judges declared Savolainen the winner. Japan protested, and as a result, the judges accepted the Japanese protest and changed the verdict to Nakano’s victory. Also, in the match between Li Guihuan of Japan and Spio of Finland, Spio's quick punch hit Li's head, causing Li to lose his balance and sway. Spio seized the opportunity to attack fiercely, and Li fell to the ground again. From the second round onwards, Li recovered his strength and continued to compete. However, due to falling in the first round, he was declared the loser.

Our Entire Army Was Defeated; The Reason Was Arriving in Germany Too Late; Exhaustion from the Journey Prevented Recovery of Strength; Hoping the Countrymen Will Strive to Erase Today's Shame; Basketball Tournament Enters Fourth Week 147

Berlin, August 11th, via Wireless Broadcast. Yesterday's basketball games included four matches: (1) Poland vs. Latvia, halftime score 14-12, final score 28-23, Poland wins; (2) Mexico vs. Egypt, halftime score 16-8, final score 32-10, Mexico wins; (3) Brazil vs. China, halftime score 16-5, final score 32-14, Brazil wins; (4) Czechoslovakia vs. Germany, halftime score 11-6, final score 20-9, Czechoslovakia wins. Therefore, Poland, Brazil, Mexico, and Czechoslovakia have entered the third week. Today's schedule is (1) Estonia vs. Philippines, (2) Chile vs. Italy, (3) Mexico vs. Japan, (4) Sweden vs. Canada, (5) Czechoslovakia vs. Uruguay, (6) Poland vs. Brazil. The United States has a bye. The winners will advance to the fourth week, and the losers will compete against each other again. In yesterday's basketball game between China and Brazil, the Brazilian team's skills were quite good, especially the center, who was the most excellent. Whether it was long shots or close-range shots under the basket, they were all successful. Therefore, Brazil's victory yesterday must be attributed to the center. Conversely, our team was the complete opposite. Not only were long shots unsuccessful, but also close-range shots under the basket did not go in. It seemed that all the players could not exert their strength. Lack of training was one of the reasons, but physical inferiority was indeed a major factor in the failure. As a result, we lost with a score of 14-32. In other competitions, we were also completely defeated. Overall, our country's participation in this World Games can be said to be a complete defeat. The reason was that we arrived in Germany too late. The athletes were exhausted from the long journey, and their physical strength could not be restored. After arriving in Germany, they were not acclimatized to the environment, which affected their health. Therefore, they could not compete with other countries. The most fundamental reason was the lack of physical strength, training, and experience. Compared with other countries, the gap was vast. This is greatly related to the health of the nation. However, it is somewhat comforting that although the football team lost to England, all parties praised them highly. The basketball team was also able to fight fiercely in several games, leaving a deep impression on various countries. Therefore, this trip cannot be said to be a complete failure. However, compared with our neighboring country Japan, the difference is immeasurable. It is hoped that the countrymen will work hard to strengthen their bodies in the future to erase today's shame.
