On the Deck of the Kontor Float (5) From Bombay to Madenwa 160

— Special Correspondent for this Newspaper Yu Yi Sends

Around 2 PM on July 9th, after arriving in Bombay, India, since there was a six-hour stopover, the team members split into groups, three to five in a group, and went ashore to various places to visit, to relieve the boredom of sea life. Those who boarded the ship from Bombay included Li Huitang, Bao Jiaping, Huang Jiliang, Li Tiansheng, Tan Jiangbai, Mai Shaohan, Cai Wenli, Huang Meiyi, Xu Yahui, Chen Zhenhe, Li Guowei, Liang Rongzhao, Liang Shutang, Zheng Jiliang, Yang Shuiyi, Zhuo Shijin, Feng Jinxiang, Zhang Xianyuan, Sun Jinshun, Ye Beihua, Cao Guicheng, and Jia Youliang, 24 members of our country's World Games football delegation who had fought in various parts of Southeast Asia for a long time, as well as director Rong Qizhao and manager Huang Jiajun. Coach Yan Chengkun will remain in the port, and it is heard that he will take a plane to Berlin in the near future. Our football team fought against the Bombay Essence Team on July 8, resulting in a 3-3 draw. According to local Western newspapers, our team's attacking and defending connection technology cooperation is above Bombay's, especially Li Huitang, Cao Guicheng, and Sun Jinshun, who performed well, but the opponent's defense was tight, and our team was tired from the journey, so we were unable to deeply wound the enemy. After the floating platform left Bombay at 8:00 PM on the 9th, it encountered storms when it lingered in the Arabian Sea on the 9th, 10th, and 11th for three days, and the vibrations were quite strong. More than half of the team members suffered from seasickness, and all activities were temporarily suspended. It was not until noon on the 13th that things calmed down, and the team began to resume their activities. The Weiqi championship competition began at 10:00 AM on July 13th, with more than ten participants including Hao Gengsheng, Feng Youzhen, Li Zhou, Qian Yiqin, Wang Shoufang, and Liu Yunzhang. The final was held on July 18th, with Wang Shoufang having the highest voice for the championship.

The study group has held many meetings and has now decided on the study direction. In addition to holding student camps and recreational meetings at this World Games, there is also a "Sports Conference." The agenda of the Sports Conference and an outline of the study direction are recorded below (see Appendices 1 and 2).

Around 3:00 PM on July 14th, we arrived at Massawa Port in Italian Africa. The journey from Bombay to here is 2,080 miles.

Outline of the Study Direction of the Study Group 161

(1) Administration: 1. Administrative system (central, local), 2. Teacher training, 3. Teacher assessment, treatment, and control, 4. Goals and methods (future trends), 5. Funding (sources and expenses), 6. Inspection and guidance, 7. Standard test methods, (2) School Sports: 1. Facilities and organization, 2. Teaching and training (curriculum, teaching materials, standards, special skills, etc.), 3. Extracurricular activities (intra-school, inter-school competitions, etc.), 4. Differences between men's and women's sports facilities, 5. Student living conditions and their training management.

(3) Social Sports: 1. Facilities and organization (children, youth, adults, elderly) (public sports fields, public gymnasiums, swimming pools, etc.), 2. Guidance and training (training in special sports skills), 3. Popular sports, 4. Industrial sports, 5. Organization and work of various sports associations, (4) Other: 1. Propositions of sports leaders of various countries, 2. Status of sports journalism, 3. Organization and facilities for youth training, 4. Situation of youth labor services, 5. Organization and facilities for military and police sports, 6. Public awareness of sports in various countries, 7. Background of sports in various countries (economic, political, environmental, etc.), 8. Sports research undertakings, 9. Manufacturing of sports equipment, 10. Hygiene, 11. Health education.

The study group tentatively plans to edit the following visiting reports: 1. World Games (including preparation), 2. Recreation Conference, 3. Sports Student Association, 4. Sports Conference, 5. Sports Medicine Conference, 6. Various performances (gymnastics, dance, folk games, etc.), 7. Various exhibitions (sculpture, music, etc.), 8. Tours (scenery and culture), (Note) It is best to attach photos to each report. Team members organize a photography team.

(6) From Massawa to Venice

Arrived in Massawa around 3:00 PM on July 14th. Massawa is an important town in Italian Eritrea, Africa, and was a key transportation route for the Italian army during the invasion of Abyssinia. The entire town is very small. Aside from the stationed Italian army, there is no trade and nothing worth seeing. Several hundred Italian soldiers boarded the ship from here, presumably returning home in triumph. The weather in Africa is extremely hot, and quite a few passengers on the ship fell ill. Three Westerners died on the ship while passing through the seas. Several members of our delegation also became sick, with Wu Bixian's condition being more serious. Fortunately, he fully recovered after four days. Due to the accompanying doctor's inability to fulfill his duties, many members of the delegation became ill. It is regrettable that they had to voluntarily pay for medical treatment from the ship's doctor.

The floating platform arrived at Port Said at 3:00 PM on July 17th. Except for a very few members who joined the China Travel Service's organized tour of Cairo, Egypt, and disembarked at Suez, the rest of us stayed on the ship to pass through the canal. Although this port of Said is small, it is quite clean and tidy. Many members of the delegation purchased Egyptian products and returned to the ship. The ship set sail directly for Italy at 7:00 PM that afternoon. At 10:00 AM on July 18th, our delegation held a plenary meeting, chaired by Shen Siliang. It was said that countries must first become members of the World Games Federation in order to participate. The organization of the Games is actually composed of various international sports federations. Any country wishing to participate in a particular sport must first become a member of the international federation for that sport. The World Games Federation has a committee, and it is a great honor that Mr. Wang Zhengting, our country's representative, is also an official of that organization. This time, our country is participating in seven events: (1) Athletics, (2) Basketball, (3) Football, (4) Weightlifting, (5) Swimming, (6) Cycling, (7) Art. Our country had already joined the above-mentioned international sports federations in advance. The significance of our delegation's participation in this World Games is as follows: (1) From the perspective of the inspection team, its mission is to learn from others' strengths and make up for its own shortcomings. (2) From the perspective of the athletes, our country's athletes in general are quite arrogant and conceited. They need to learn humbly and must not think that running and jumping is the end of it. They must take the initiative to learn. Even after the Games are over, they must continue to work hard to practice. Ma Dehan gave a speech, roughly saying that we are "representatives." The word "representative" means responsibility, duty. You must understand what you represent. (1) Others see a representative as representing all Chinese people. (2) When dealing with competition referees and perceived injustices, never lose your temper. Pay attention to spiritual cultivation and have "youthful spirit." The so-called youthful spirit is (1) agility, (2) liveliness, (3) spirit of service, (4) discipline. We, as instructors, administrators, and athletes, should all "love our country." At the very least, "what I do should not disgrace my country." Hao Gengsheng said (1) We can fail in skills, but we must never fail in spirit. Even if we lose, we must lose honorably and show that our country has promise. (2) Remember not to let people make fun of us, because enemies and friends alike will expose our weaknesses and let people all over the world know. (3) We must have national consciousness. When Chinese people learn from others' strengths, we must not forget that we are Chinese. It is truly commendable that we can still go abroad to compete when the domestic situation is so difficult. Each representative should pay attention to (1) protecting your own body, (2) maintaining the spirit of a great Chinese citizen, (3) preparing to fight for the country in the international arena.

The German consultant, Kautz, then delivered a speech to welcome our delegation, translated by Ms. Mei Fuxiang. He roughly said that soon we will arrive in Berlin, Germany, and the people of all of Germany are very honored to be able to receive such an excellent Chinese delegation. I (Kautz speaking of himself) take this opportunity to represent the German government and its leaders in expressing twelve points of sincerity in welcoming you all. I believe that the German people will do their best to ensure that your stay is a great success and comfort. However, if there are any shortcomings, please consider the great difficulties that Germany is undertaking for this conference. In Berlin alone, there were originally four million residents, and it is expected that there will be eight million guests from various countries attending this World Games. You must know that the wishes of the German people are purely good. From the lowest person on the street to the highest leader, all will do their best to satisfy guests from all countries, without a doubt. This sentiment is especially directed towards our Chinese friends. The relationship between China and Germany has always been friendly. All Germans who have lived in China and returned to their country cannot forget your great nation. The German people are striving to deepen the friendship between the two countries. This time, your country has sent such a fine delegation to Germany, which can be said to be the beginning of a historical era. Your country's culture is superior, which is not only deeply understood by Germany, but also known to all of Europe. Therefore, it increases the responsibility that you bear for your country's people and nation. Not only the people of Germany, but also the people of the world are watching closely at this time. Therefore, even the slightest of your actions is related to the reputation of your country and people. May you not fail the mission of your country in sending you to Germany, bring glory to the country, and open your eyes, then honor and victory, perhaps there will be, perhaps there will not be, but success ultimately belongs to you and your country. After the speech, Xu Minhui led everyone in cheering before dismissing the meeting. The delegation's Go (Weiqi) championship, organized by the Entertainment Committee, has been underway since July 13th. All contestants have been competing in an orderly manner. The final between Feng Youzhen and Wang Shoufang took place on July 18th. As a result, Wang won the championship with a score of two to one.

In recent days, the inspection team has held multiple meetings and has properly assigned personnel to each group to facilitate future inspections. The list of personnel in each group is as follows:

(Administrative Group) Wu Bangwei, Li Zhou, Xu Yingchao, Xu Minhui, Fu Jingru, Zhang Huilan, Shao Rugan. Secretary: Xu Minhui. (Conveners) Wu Bangwei, Shao Rugan. (Conveners) Peng Wenyu, Yao Xianqu, Chen Yongsheng. (Social Group) Jiang Liangui, Yu Yongzuo, Jiang Zhende, Ye Guanwan, Zhao Wenzao, Qian Yiqin, Du Yufei, Huang Yunzhi. (Secretary) Qian Yiqin. Three Short-Term Treatments for Premature Ejaculation 175

— Yao Erchang, MD, University of Pennsylvania, USA

……The three categories of cerebral, spinal cord, and peripheral, and their treatments……A thorough understanding of the fundamental treatments and points to note……An overview of the harms of premature ejaculation and the pain suffered by the partner.

Premature ejaculation is a functional neurological disorder, but it is different from neurasthenic impotence. Hypersensitivity of the ejaculatory nerve center and the conduction glands is the cause of this disease. The main factors that contribute to this cause are entirely due to systemic nutritional disorders, or bad habits of masturbation during the developmental period, and congenital deficiencies and acquired maladjustments. It can also occur when other serious illnesses have not fully recovered, or from opium or morphine poisoning. Therefore, treatment must pay attention to each of these causes and the method of fundamental eradication.

(1) Symptoms of Cerebral Premature Ejaculation

This type of premature ejaculation occurs in the first stage of neurasthenic impotence. The erectile center of the spinal cord is damaged. When an erection is not sufficient or there is no erection at all, the ejaculatory center becomes excited first, resulting in the act of ejaculation.

According to the ordinary phenomenon, the erectile center is extremely excited first, which then causes the excitation of the ejaculatory center, and then there is the act of ejaculation. However, when the erectile center is damaged, it is not yet excited, but the ejaculatory center becomes excited first, resulting in ejaculation. At this time, if the excitation of the mental center is added, the phenomenon becomes even more severe, even leading to nocturnal emissions without an erection during the day. This type is called cerebral premature ejaculation.

(2) The Pathway of Spinal Cord Premature Ejaculation

Early ejaculation, in addition to the above, can also be caused by the action of the mind, that is, when strong sexual concepts are felt in the brain, the stimulation of the senses can also excite the ejaculatory center, resulting in premature ejaculation, which is also a common occurrence.

(3) Peripheral Premature Ejaculation

The cause of peripheral premature ejaculation is mostly swelling and hypersensitivity of the seminal vesicles. The inflammation of the seminal vesicles is mostly due to masturbation, or contracting gonorrhea during intercourse. The inflammation of the seminal vesicles then harms the ejaculatory center. Among the above types of premature ejaculation, the most effective treatment is the method of supplementing the reproductive glands. At this time, "Reproductive Essence" should be taken, which will revitalize the body and replenish energy, and the partner can deeply gain a strong sense of pleasure. Commercial News

Grains: Japanese Still Buying Wheat 176

Yesterday's wheat market was generally flat after the opening in the morning. Although the price of foreign wheat continued to fall sharply, the demand for spot wheat from factories suddenly became active, unlike the dullness of the previous week. The goods were also purchased at higher prices, and the Japanese traders also made transactions every day, which made people more confident. Therefore, although the price of foreign wheat was slightly lower, the market atmosphere remained stable. Only the prices for this month to November were slightly lower by one cent, and the prices for December and January were also flat at the beginning. Then, as buying interest increased, the prices rebounded by three cents. According to the current trend, it is difficult to predict a decline in the short term. The spot wheat market was active due to the mutual buying interest of factories and Japanese traders, and the demand was very strong. Each supplier secretly raised prices by five cents. Chen wheat from Yaowan was quoted at four yuan and ninety cents, Zhangbaling Yaowan wheat at four yuan and ninety cents, Jiehe wheat at four yuan and ninety-five cents, Gaoyou wheat at four yuan and seventy cents, Wuhu wheat at four yuan and sixty-eight cents, second-grade at six cents, Wuyi wheat at four yuan and seventy-eight cents, Yangzhou wheat at four yuan and fifty-five cents, Shiying wheat at four yuan and sixty-seven or eight cents, Liuhe wheat at four yuan and sixty-seven, eight, or nine cents, Huaian wheat at four yuan and seventy cents, Hankou wheat at four yuan and sixty-eight cents, settled at six cents, second-grade at five cents. Fuxin purchased 10,000 bags, Fufeng purchased 9,000 bags, and Shenda purchased 3,000 bags. It is said that the highest-quality goods have been sold to the Japanese traders for five yuan.

The Future of the Flour Market Still Holds Changes 177

Yesterday's flour market showed a trend of softening first and then rising. The price of foreign wheat in Chicago continued to fall by forty or fifty cents, and in Canada, the near-term fell by one yuan and the far-term fell by ninety-seven cents. Therefore, people were very calm when the prices opened. The opening price for this month was only one cent and two points, and the prices for September to December were also slightly lower by one or two points. However, the price for January did not fall but rose instead. Therefore, after the opening of these two rounds of trading, people's confidence immediately rose. At that time, actual sales customers from the north and south also traded spot flour, and futures were also being purchased, so people's confidence suddenly became firm, jumping by two or three points compared to the initial round. After the third round, the prices were relatively flat, and buying and selling transactions were still active. According to estimates by those in the industry, the market value of foreign wheat is difficult to agree on for the time being. If they gradually approach, there will be huge changes in the future.

Yesterday, the British company's "Sumandri" steamer set sail for Europe with 4,000 bags of flour destined for Singapore. The reporter heard this and considered that flour exports have been rare in recent years. I made a special inquiry, and the company stated that flour exports have indeed been rare recently, but they were common during the European war twenty years ago. This is the first time for this export, and it is feared that there will be more in the future. It is also heard that several thousand more bags will be shipped to Medan, Dutch East Indies, tomorrow.

Special Article Answering Mr. Dong Yuncong of Hangzhou 195

(1) The prices of wheat, peanuts, sesame, etc., published in the newspaper are all in units of 100 market catties and are calculated inclusive of the bag.

(2) Regarding the market prices of various goods, such as wheat, which is currently in the new crop season, there are daily market prices. Peanuts, sesame, etc., are sometimes available and sometimes not. Market price increases and decreases are based purely on whether buying and selling can come close and what the inventory is like. There are no specialized publications for these goods. If you want to understand, you can refer to the commercial section of this newspaper, which is published daily.

(3) Regarding the issue of selling goods, all wheat and other goods shipped to Shanghai must be entrusted to miscellaneous grain merchants for resale. Their handling commission is 1% of the total price of the goods. As for the Flour Association and the Miscellaneous Grain Association, they are places for gatherings of the respective industries and do not accept consignment sales in principle. Even flour factories, apart from self-operation, distant customer goods are handled by miscellaneous grain merchants, and there are no direct transactions. In general, entrusting merchants to sell goods can be pre-designated, or sold upon arrival of the goods, or sold at a limited price. The merchants will follow the customer's intentions. This method of entrustment can be done by letter or telegram. Therefore, once a merchant is entrusted, problems such as unfamiliarity with the area and difficulty in promoting sales are readily solved.

(4) One market catty is equal to half a kilogram.

(5) After the arrival of through transport goods, they are naturally stored in the railway warehouse. Warehouse rent is collected after five days. However, the railway warehouse is slightly larger than the bank's storage area. Merchants who accept entrustment can arrange for transshipment. As for freight, it can be paid at the delivery station or at the arrival station. Bank warehouse fees are four cents per bag per month. If it is less than one month, it is also calculated as one month.

(6) There are currently no taxes on wheat, peanuts, sesame, etc.

(7) For freight, if the railway through transport is used, there should be rules at the delivery station that can be inquired about nearby. If you entrust a transfer company to transport, from a practical point of view, it will be slightly higher than railway through transport. This can be discussed and compared with the local railway or transfer company.

(8) Shipping losses are unavoidable. If you entrust through transport, it is relatively less troublesome and leakage may be slightly less.

(9) Unloading fees After the goods arrive in Shanghai, unloading the car and entering the warehouse costs two jiao per ton. The same applies when leaving the warehouse.

(10) For bulk transportation, regardless of the quantity, the railway has regulations and there are no preferential treatments. A full carload is 40 tons, and other tons can also be consigned, but it is more difficult to consolidate cars.

(10) (1) Transportation and sales, of course, various goods can be transported and sold to various places, but you still need to entrust local merchants. For example, after the goods arrive in Shanghai, there must be a merchant to receive the bill of lading before they can be sold. For goods from afar, you can pledge at a local bank, between 60% and 70% of the market price of the goods. The remaining payment will be remitted by the handling merchant after the goods are sold. In addition to receiving a 1% commission, the handling merchant is also responsible for overdue warehouse rent, loading and unloading fees, transfer fees, insurance fees, sales weighing fees, and pledge interest remittance fees, telegraphic fees.

(10) (2) Loading time: After various goods are shipped by the starting station, if there are no special circumstances, there should be a scheduled arrival time. It takes about four or five days to load from your place to Shanghai. However, it is difficult to predetermine whether the goods can get a freight car immediately at the starting station.

(10) (3) As for the trend of market prices, the so-called morning and evening are different and it is difficult to predict, because the various items listed are related to international trade. You can check the daily commercial information in this newspaper, and you will be able to infer from one thing to another. If you want to know the exact market price of the item, you may wish to send a sample to this newspaper, and we will be happy to introduce someone in the industry to clarify the real situation, so that you know the difference between good quality and ordinary, and you cannot purely use market prices as a standard.

Spring and Autumn

Tidbits 196

— (Yao Mingran)

Sour plum soup is like people competing for face, superficially well-dressed, but in fact, it is full of holes inside. That sour and sweet taste is just like the sour plum soup of the old capital of Beiping!

When a round watermelon is divided, I think of the future re-division of the world's colonies, isn't it the same?

People fanning fans give off a graceful air, just like a benefactor in the summer, but once it gets cool, they have to retire!

Ice cream, Hōlan water, shaved ice are like heroes of an era, who are forgotten once they lose power. Peaches are like women with different styles, graceful in demeanor. Lotus leaves and lotus flowers stand gracefully in the center of the water in summer. Looking at them, it's like taking a refreshing medicine, like a refined scholar, free and easy, making people eliminate all worldly worries!

Tight Lotus Breeze, Cool Moon Rising 197

— Lake Beggar

The coolness of West Lake in June is only in the deep night. During the day, the water vapor rises, causing stifling heat that does not dissipate. Those floating waves licking the shore are all due to the hot wind. The furnace pants for breath, and the palm-leaf fan is useless. Only those who have lived here for a long time can understand this suffering. The lake is a lotus root swamp, red smiling and white weeping, most beautiful in midsummer, but confined by the scorching sun, it is pitiful to see it wilt in the middle of the day. Therefore, I once wrote in a miscellaneous poem: "Ten thousand trees suffer from heat and cry, a wisp of fragrance sustains the lake and mountain's life." Towards evening, fireflies glow red, and there is a slight coolness in the Wushan area. But the wind on the lake still makes people feel sick in bursts, so living in a floating boat, you must wait for the dew to nourish the grass and the midnight bell to ring clearly in the forest. Because the dew is heavy, the residual heat lingers, and the moon rises and the hidden heat dissipates. At that time, the chaotic mountains stretch their heads, the wind blowing through the trees sends coolness, and ten thousand lotus flowers straighten their backs, sharing fragrance and shaking green. It feels as if the surrounding clouds and water all understand human intentions. The lake is clear and fertile, as transparent as a琉璃瓶 (glass bottle?), with red and white flowers growing in a chaotic mix, like a natural masterpiece of 清供 (pure offering?). Besides the solitary guest, there are also those who bring their families and whisper among the翠盖 (green canopies), looking like nothing less than immortals. "Clouds embrace, quiet and without a sound, it is the night to raft on the Silver River. Thirty-six mandarin ducks under the moon, fragrant saliva falling into the water activates the lotus flowers." I am used to drifting and have erased my delusions. But carefully appreciating the pure plants, I suddenly feel a sense of sorrow: I have always said that the lotus is the gentleman of flowers, and it can also be compared to a short-lived talent. The appearance is beautiful, and the heart is full of bitterness. It blooms and withers in a summer, who is it for? Thinking of the ignorance of things, it moves my sadness even more. The wind is tight on the萍末 (duckweed ends?), and the accumulated dew falls like tears. Taking advantage of the sparse stars hanging the oars, the 葛薄 (thin kudzu cloth?) seems unable to withstand the cold.

White Hair 198

— Junmei

After discovering a single white hair for the first time, I want to lament that the days are numbered and feel that I am getting old and dying, although I am not yet thirty years old, but the past years are like a dream in an instant.

Running around and shouting all day long, jumping like a dog, calling like a cat, thinking, depressed, calculating for a family's food, clothing, and shelter, white hairs will grow out one by one without end. Those who have tea in hand, food in mouth, embracing charming wives and concubines, without a thought in their heads, and no scheming, the white hairs do not dare to show themselves at all. It not only teases people, but also is very snobbish.

There are famous white hairs in history, one is Wu Zixu from the Li State period, who was so anxious after stealing through Zhaoguan overnight that his beard and hair turned white, and the other is Wang Lang, from the Three Kingdoms period, who was scolded to death by Zhuge Liang for being a "old thief with gray beard and an old man with white hair!" The former, because of his white hair, later established many great undertakings, avenged his father and brothers, and created the temporary strength of the Wu State, while the latter could not bear the scolding of white hair and sacrificed his life alive.

The transformation of hair into white and the role of nerves are indeed very related. After Louis XVI's queen received the death sentence, she was so depressed that her golden hair turned white by the next day. This is a famous historical fact. Also, in a certain place in Germany, a woman had her hair and eyebrows turn white because of excessive panic when a house collapsed. So, Wu Zixu's hair turning white overnight does not seem to be entirely unfounded.

Qing Dynasty, Qian Muzhai married Liu Rushi, one with grizzled white hair and the other with a bright red face, quite like an old cow eating young grass, but the two were very fond of each other. One day, Muzhai stared at Rushi, and Rushi asked, "Why do you love me?" He said, "I love your black hair and white face, so why do you love me?" Rushi said, "I love your white hair and black face." Unexpectedly, white hair, after thousands of years, actually got a confidante of a generation of beauties, and did not do little to give voice to the white hair.

A Badge of Shame 201

— Cheng Zhenru

This year's summer, following the shifts between storms and strong sunlight, alternates between coolness and heat. This symbolizes the warmth and coldness of human emotions, offering young people entering society for the first time a most obvious lesson.

In the past couple of days, the mercury in thermometers has been rising again, soon approaching one hundred degrees. Consequently, the number of bare-chested people has also increased. Although going shirtless is a bad habit of our people, the discomfort of laborers when they get hot is just as unbearable as a wealthy person urgently needing to relieve themselves but being denied access to a toilet.

Liyang is located at the center of the Beijing-Hangzhou National Highway. The administrative authorities are vigorously promoting the New Life Movement. Naturally, going shirtless must be prohibited. Persuasion might not be effective, and punishment seems too harsh. Therefore, they adopted a stamping method. Police officers, carrying ink and a "Shame" stamp, patrol the streets. When they encounter shirtless individuals, they stamp the words "Shame" on their skin. This is carried out swiftly and decisively, and the display of semi-naked bodies has decreased somewhat. However, some bewildered villagers perceive this as an insult and have started conflicts. At the same time, stores selling Guang-style goods reported a shortage of undershirts and tank tops.

Someone jokingly said that stamping the "Shame" mark on shirtless people is somewhat similar to tax collectors stamping "Inspected" on pork. However, laborers, torn between caring for their shame and needing to eat, have no choice but to save money on food and spend it on clothing, buying a tank top to wear, which ends up soaked in sweat all day long, with no way to avoid it.

Police officers, while chasing shirtless individuals to stamp them, overheard the sound of mahjong tiles from a rice shop upstairs and unintentionally caught gamblers. This is another amusing incident caused by the stamping campaign. It shows that some of our people still have leisure time and know how to enjoy themselves.

Ping Pong Opera in Shanghai 202

The birthplace of Ping Pong Opera is in Rehe, but its popularity lies in Shenyang. Therefore, the melodies of Ping Pong Opera are most pleasing to the taste of people from outside the Great Wall. The Ping Pong Opera venues in Shenyang are always packed with listeners every day.

Since Zhang Zuolin entered the customs, the Feng army has been stationed all over Pingjin. To cater to the Communists, Pingjin has Ping Pong Opera theaters. In the past, Ping Pong Opera was very simple. Except for the lead actress, there were not as many supporting roles as there are now. After invading Pingjin, it gradually improved. The plays performed also became complete stories, roughly forming a scale.

The southward invasion of the Ping Pong Opera force came to Shanghai. The first was the Zhu Baoxia and Zhuxia sisters, performing at the New World Hotel. It was also because of the exquisite skills of Baoxia and Zhuxia that they received praise from people in Shanghai. Ping Pong Opera in Shanghai has a superior position like today, so the Zhu sisters are the only heroes to promote Ping Pong Opera to Shanghai.

After Zhu Baoxia left, the Ping Pong female actors who came to Shanghai were Furonghua, Ailianjun, Bai Yushuang, Zhang Cailan, Yu Lingzhi, and Xicaiyun, who came to Shanghai recently. Although each person’s acting skills are commendable, compared with the color and skills of Zhu Baoxia, it always feels that there is a difference between a small witch and a big witch. This is a sign that Zhu's talent and skills are better than others.

Now, the power of Ping Pong Opera has almost filled Shanghai. No major amusement park does not regard Ping Pong Opera as a pioneer to attract tourists. The Great World occupies the top spot, sparing no expense, and hired the Zhu Baoxia Zhuxia sisters. Xianshi Amusement Park, Yu Lingzhi, Zhang Cailan, and Bai Yushuang also said that they will come again in the autumn. Recently, Xicailian has come to Shanghai and auditioned on the Tianchan Stage. There is no doubt that the Ping Pong teams in Shanghai have surpassed Pingjin. Among these Ping Pong female corners, their acting skills, except for Xicailian, have been seen by Shanghainese, and the following comments can be obtained.

The plays performed by Bai Yushuang are only of the kind of Ma Widow's Shop, Indecent Mirror, Pan Jinlian, and Yan Xijiao. The rest of the actors are not first-class talents among the Ping Pong female actors. The most satisfying one is naturally Zhu Shixia. Her expressions, singing skills, joy, anger, sorrow, and happiness are all excellent. Sometimes when performing lewd plays, she can also be happy without being obscene, and the implications are endless. Therefore, Zhu has fascinated many audiences in Shanghai.

Xicailian, who is coming now, has not seen her color and skills by Shanghainese. It is said that she is very qualified, and her age is only second to Bai Yushuang, and the older one is between twenty-seven and eight. Her husband, named Li Xiaofang, sings on the same stage and never leaves. If the Tianchan trial performance has the power to call, it may be possible to enter the Dasing Amusement Park.

Japanese Children's Toys 203

— Ji Yun

Toys are children's treasures, and no child dislikes them. Japan's toy industry has already occupied the first place in the world. Eighty to ninety percent of the toys purchased by children in our country are Japanese goods. The Japanese themselves also say that no matter how much countries around the world increase tariff barriers or exclude Japanese goods, innocent children only know that they are fun and have no economic or political effect. The reason why Japanese toys can be popular around the world is that their toys can grasp the psychology of children. Now, the most popular Japanese toys are militarized things, which is also due to the environment. Airplanes, tanks, and guns, imperceptibly make children's psychology gradually have a tendency to like war, and only know how to obey and believe in the Emperor of the Motherland. Most of these toys are made of tinplate, which is very similar to the real thing, and is rotated by springs. Tanks and guns are equipped with calcium carbide, which can emit light and sound. Although the wooden ones cannot move, they are not easily damaged and are cheaper. Our country often wants to imitate Japanese toys, and Japan also imitates our country's toys such as bamboo dragons and sound-producing cicadas, and then transports them to the South Pacific Islands.

Celluloid dolls and rattles are toys for three- or four-year-old babies, and not as popular as tinplate toys that can make sounds and move automatically. Rubber-made cattle and horses are gradually decreasing in sales, and our country can also manufacture them. The value of toys exceeding one yuan is not very suitable. Things that cost a dime or two, on the other hand, can be popular everywhere. The toys made in our country are large in price, and the types of products are small, and it is still difficult to compete with Japanese goods. All parts of Japan have local toys, using shells and conch shells to make stationery toys, which has also become a sideline.

Japanese children can have many cheap picture books, which are all materials of militarism. Such as the stories of the Russo-Japanese War and the Sino-Japanese War, as well as ideal pictures of future wars. Therefore, Japanese children's loyalty to the emperor and patriotism does not fall behind adults. These kinds of pictorials already have Chinese explanations and will be promoted in the three eastern provinces and North China. Another kind is attached with the native language of the South Pacific, which is specially sold in the area of the South Pacific Islands. Parents who care for children should pay attention to the implications of toys when purchasing toys, and it is appropriate to contain educational significance. On the one hand, I hope that toy companies will manufacture toys that meet our current needs, and do not specialize in blind imitation to satisfy themselves.

Chen Jitang's Taboo Number Thirteen 205

— Me

After Chen Jitang stepped down, he originally lived at No. 13 Mai Chang Nu Road. Chen believed that Western customs tabooed the number 13, so at 3 pm on the 8th, he moved to the Buddhist Association in Li Garden with Chen Weizhou, Mo Xiuying, and others. In fact, Chen was originally unlucky, so he went to live at No. 13 Mai Chang Nu Road. It was not because he lived at No. 13 that he was unlucky. Therefore, what relationship does the number 13 or 14 have with the luck or misfortune of personnel matters?

The unlucky number of thirteen also has this saying in our country. The thirteenth and twenty-first days of the first month are Yang Gong's taboo days. If a son is born on this day, he will definitely beg for food. This is the unlucky number of thirteen. The patterns of tortoise shells also have thirteen sections, so people often use thirteen pieces as a source of ridicule. In fact, the spirit turtle has existed for a thousand years, why is it an evil thing? Even if it is born on the thirteenth day of the first month, and the result is not begging for food, this is everywhere. There are more people who are not born on the thirteenth day of the first month, but specialize in begging for food as a way of life. The depth of our people's superstition can be seen from this.

Therefore, Chen Jitang's misfortune has nothing to do with No. 13. Chen Jitang's first major misfortune was that he did not accept the orders of the central government and became a separatist situation. The second major misfortune was that he plundered the people's wealth and made all of it his personal property. The third major misfortune was that he imposed exorbitant taxes and cruelly treated our people. The fourth major misfortune was that he listened to rumors and was arrogant. Chen Jitang's misfortune lies in the above four things, what does it have to do with No. 13?

The most ridiculous thing is that Chen, as a Chinese person, believes in Western superstition, which is even more foolish. Assuming that Indian and South Pacific customs include bowing to crows and kneeling to long snakes, will Chen follow their customs? There are more houses with the number 13 in this city than anywhere else. There are 13 roads and 13 alleys. I have never heard of a house with the number 13 being uninhabited, nor have I heard of anything unlucky after living there.

In short, Chen Jitang's downfall this time was due to superstition. After the downfall, the idea of superstition has not been eliminated, and it is still superstition. Chen is really a man who does not wake up until his death. And the next day's telegram said that Chen Jitang had taken a foreign ship to go abroad, then the saying that No. 13 is unlucky was originally a false name, just to take this opportunity to slip away. However, Chen was originally a cunning old fox, and he deceived the eyes of the world a lot.

A Visit to the Puyi Vocational Training Institute (Part 2) 206

— Fang Zhou

Apprentices in the institute cannot request to leave the institute without a reason, nor can they leave the institute a step without permission. If they want to go to the back to urinate or defecate, they must also obtain a certificate before being allowed to go out. However, if they are sick, they are also allowed to take leave and be taken back by their family members for treatment. Apprentices who are sick are sent to the hospital if they are seriously ill, and if they are nearby, they are asked to seek medical treatment in the institute and notify their family members.

The procedure for entering the institute is extremely simple. As long as they are poor children between the ages of twelve and sixteen, they can request to enter the institute, but they must be really poor and able to find a substantial guarantor in this city to be qualified. However, the institute has a fixed quota, and when the quota is full, the institute can reject the request.

The administrator, Mr. Xing, talked with me for a long time in the reception room. I looked up and saw a portrait of Mr. Shi Liangcai on the wall. After Mr. Shi passed away, a sum of money was transferred to the institute.

After the class bell in the workshop rang, Mr. Xing accompanied me to visit each department for a week. The first is the metalworking department, which is a manufacturing plant for machine parts and materials. There are dozens of motors there, and each motor has three or four apprentices working next to it. In addition, there is also a technician and several teaching assistants to guide and teach. The second is the electrical materials department, which produces lead money feet, round wood, and box boards. The third is the clay sculpture department. There are more than a dozen apprentices carving various clay figures in the models; some are making hand-mounted feet, some are opening their faces and drawing eyebrows, some are applying powder and oil, and some are adding beards and matching clothes. Everyone is working together. It is said that the mud they use is also shipped from Wuxi. The fourth is the bamboo ware department, and the products here are various bamboo wares of different thicknesses. The fifth is the rattan ware department. In addition to rattan beds and rattan chairs, there are also modern rattan appliances. The sixth is the sewing department, which specializes in making clothes for the apprentices in the institute and small clothes for the clay figures. The seventh is the mounting department, which specializes in mounting paintings and other works. The eighth is the Western music department, which is in a room upstairs and studies for only two hours a day.

The classrooms for Chinese, arithmetic, and bookkeeping are upstairs. Their highest grade is the sixth grade, but the level is uneven, because some of the apprentices who enter the institute already have high school levels, while others are illiterate. The teachers in the institute can only take on some ordinary courses.

After visiting these places, Mr. Xing led me to visit the dining room, bedroom, and storage room.

The bedroom is upstairs, and it is a large floor with one hundred and forty single iron beds arranged. The air and light are very sufficient. A small room outside is for people with infectious diseases to live in. Further forward is the bedroom for the staff. Next to the classroom is the storage room, which is full of clothes for the apprentices.

The dining room is in the back; this dining room is very large, and it is enough to accommodate more than a hundred people eating at the same time. Next to it is a tiger stove.

The air in the whole institute is very good. The open spaces everywhere are full of flowers and trees, especially on several wisteria frames, which are covered with green grapes, which is very cute.

When I left, I asked Mr. Xing for a copy of the institute's charter.

Apprentice Xiaowei 207

— Rui Fa

"You little devil, you are not careful when doing things, can you eat? If you get burned to death, no one will care. You little pig..."

Xiaowei, an apprentice at a carpenter's shop, had just finished cooking lunch. He took a water ladle to the tiger stove to make boiling water for the boss's rice. The water in the ladle was just boiled, and a stream of hot air rushed up from the lid. Xiaowei was not careful and put his hand a little bit, and the water ladle fell off the table. The hot pot of water just poured on his left foot, which aroused the boss's anger. He glared fiercely and started scolding. If he hadn't been holding a bowl of rice in his hand and eating, he might have slapped him. At this time, Xiaowei had to endure the pain, picked up the water ladle with red, round eyes and went to the tiger stove again.

Xiaowei's feet, which had frostbite in winter and scabies in summer, were poured on by such a pot of boiling water, and blisters immediately floated up. Although he secretly applied a little bit of lard in the afternoon when the boss went out to work, the lard seemed to have lost its effect in this hot weather. The blisters broke one by one, and the five little toes were swollen like pig tails. An unbearable pain went straight from the soles of his feet to his head, but he could only endure it, his small eyes filled with tears, and he dared not say a word. He still worked as usual until eleven o'clock in the evening before climbing to the reading room and lying down.

"Does it hurt? Xiaowei. Go get some medicine to apply tomorrow morning!"

The boss does not live in the shop at night. There are only Xiaowei and another apprentice, Ah Hui, who has completed his apprenticeship, in the shop. He saw Xiaowei lying on the floor crying softly like that, and sympathetically comforted him.

Xiaowei is only fourteen years old this year, and he has been an apprentice in this carpenter's shop for two years. When he first came to be an apprentice, Xiaowei's mother asked someone to intercede with the boss. Although being an apprentice will not have a good future, Xiaowei's mother still sees it as a good job. As long as the child suffers for a few more years, he can become a carpenter and earn money to support the family. Xiaowei was also happy, being an apprentice is always better than following his mother and starving.

Xiaowei came here to be an apprentice. Every day he cooks, sweeps the floor, opens and closes the shop door, buys things... Those jobs were originally done by Ah Hui. As soon as Xiaowei came, everything was passed on to him. For two years, he only watched the boss and the carpenter master doing work, but no one ever taught him how to learn this craft.

"To make a child good, you have to let him suffer more," this is the golden rule for bosses teaching apprentices, which is also the so-called philosophy of life of "enduring hardship to become a superior person." Xiaowei came to the carpenter's shop and went through two years of training, turning a fourteen-year-old child into a skinny monkey. The shadows of laughter and crying have disappeared from that small face, and it is always that blank expression.

With such two years of experience and lessons, he naturally knows how to endure being scalded on a foot like this. He got up early the next morning to work again. The foot was more swollen than yesterday, and pus was flowing, but he had to let the pain go on its own. The work will not be reduced because of this. At the same time, he has to pretend that he is not in pain in front of the boss, so as not to get another scolding from the boss. The masters asked him how his foot was? He only replied: "It's okay," but the voice of that answer was a little trembling.

That Night 208

— Zhuo Er

After finishing rehearsing a play for some children in a night school, it was almost eleven o'clock. Although I was tired and sleepy, I didn't feel anything because I was walking and talking with them. Later, they gradually smiled and said "See you tomorrow" and turned to other roads and disappeared. At that time, I really had a kind of unspeakable feeling in my heart, lonely, lonely, like an old man in his later years abandoned by happiness. I resolutely wanted to say: Can't you walk with me for a while longer? - Just a little bit, or walk a few more steps with me! But they were all smiling brightly on their faces, resolutely turning their bodies...I was tired.

Let's go, let's go by myself!

The asphalt road stretched quietly to the distant front, disappearing into the darkness. There was no commotion on the wide street, and it was as quiet as a piece of iron, and I didn't think about anything, even how to walk. Just two shoulders carrying a heavy head, walking inexplicably. Turning every street that I was familiar with, they were all wearing a cold face, as if saying: Get out! This world doesn't belong to you

What does this have to do with me? I smiled slightly.

I walked onto a gravel road, which was a road leading directly to the alley I passed through. It pricked my feet, and every time I resolutely regarded it as a kind of torture inflicted on me. The sidewalks on both sides of the road had long been occupied by the hardworking brothers as happy sleeping beds.

The closer I got to home, the more distant the road felt, and the fatigue doubled. When I got to the door, I actually felt that sleeping on the ground would be more comfortable than going upstairs and falling in the pavilion room.

I slowly and gently walked into the door.

I am glad that I did not see it wrong, there was indeed a stranger shrinking there at the entrance of the stairs "Who are you?..." I asked the man weakly, and he did not answer. At this time, I felt a bit of fear. When I realized that I did have the strength to deal with a person, I felt at ease "What are you doing?" I asked loudly, and at the same time I turned on the light

The man stood up slowly. He was a thin old man with gray hair and a beard, pale face, hunched over, and the arms exposed in his tattered clothes were so thin and trembling violently. He opened his mouth, but he couldn't say a word because of excessive panic

"Who are you looking for?"

"Boss...boss" the old man said in a trembling voice as he bowed, "I'm not a bad person,...I came here to find someone with the surname Liu,...I don't know he moved, I..." He almost knelt down. As he spoke, he lifted his clothes to show that he had not stolen anything

I knew what kind of good person he was, and I hated his despicable appearance even more. I didn't feel sorry for him at all. I was silent for a while, and ordered him in a cold voice: Get out, as long as you dare to come again..." He quickly slipped out, and I heard him running away in the alley with a thud.

Walking up the stairs, I saw at a glance that my door was open. I went in to check. A set of clothes and five dimes placed on the desk were gone. The window facing the street that I had closed was already opened.

I hurried downstairs, passed through the alley, what else was there besides dead silence?

As if in a dream, I fell into confusion. As if stepping on a pile of cotton, I ran to the street....

In the Temple of the Mountain Gorge 209

— Qi Ying

—Miscellaneous Mountain Writings, No. 2

We rushed from Xingwen County to the foot of the southern side of Dalong Mountain, and it was already dusk. On a narrow path, we watched from afar as the setting sun reflected its last rays of the day on the peaks of Dalong Mountain. We were all anxious, unsure of where we would spend the night.

Finally, we found lodging in a mountain gorge, a dilapidated monk's temple. From the outside, it looked small, but stepping through the temple's gate shocked us. The emptiness, height, and darkness made our hair stand on end. A Buddha with a blue face and fangs, more than ten feet tall, stared at us with a pair of terrifying, fierce eyes. The four of us standing before him seemed so insignificant! Looking up, we couldn't see the roof beams. The walls were blackened by years of incense smoke. There was no one in the main hall. We looked around, east and west, and no one could say a word.

After a while, a bald little monk came out from behind the main hall, looking at us with surprise and trepidation. After we told him our purpose, he led us to a room in the back courtyard. This courtyard was even more gloomy and terrifying than the main hall. In several rooms, there were large, black coffins. Looking through the small windows covered with cobwebs, each coffin had a vegetable oil lamp with a terrifying flame flickering in front of it.

The little monk brought us a pot of tea and a kerosene lamp and then left. We heard him close the door of the front room with a 'snap', leaving us alone in this large courtyard. At this moment, we couldn't help but feel frightened. It was our first time staying overnight in this ancient temple in the remote mountains and wilderness. We almost suspected that we had entered a demon's lair or a bandit zone. We sat under the dim kerosene lamp, afraid to go to bed. Old Li, the oldest and strongest among us, held a double-barreled shotgun, aiming it at the door, ready to fire if anything seemed amiss. The other two and I each tightly held a small bread knife.

Outside, a gust of wind occasionally swept through, rustling the leaves of the trees. The large courtyard was enveloped in an atmosphere of gloom and terror. From the mountain gorge, we sometimes heard frightening cries. One of us reminded us: "Listen, that's the sound of a tiger in the mountain gorge!"

Hearing this, we became even more frightened. The night was not yet deep, and the dim moonlight outside the window was just reaching the treetops. I wondered how we would get through this long, sorrowful night! Moreover, we had to travel tomorrow. Without sleep, we would be in poor spirits when climbing over the mountains early in the morning. So Old Li suggested: "Why don't we knock on the front door and ask the little monk to find us a room to stay in the front? We can give him some extra incense money tomorrow. Otherwise, sleeping in the main hall would be fine!"

We knocked on the door for more than half an hour before there was any movement inside the room. The little monk asked in a trembling voice: "Sirs, sirs, what do you want?"

After we told him why we were knocking, the little monk insisted: "Sirs, please forgive us, forgive us. Guests are not allowed to stay in the front rooms. He was almost too anxious to speak: "Our abbot has gone to Nanchang to solicit donations. He instructed us this way when he left."

We stopped knocking and pleaded with him in a gentle voice, telling him that we were good people.

"Sirs, sirs, I know you are good people," he said, a little bolder now. "A month ago, three guests robbed our temple clean. Our abbot was injured in the arm. This time, the abbot went to Nanchang both to solicit donations and to have his injury treated." His voice was close to tears: "Sirs, we really can't allow guests to stay in the front rooms. Please forgive us, forgive us."

Having no choice, we returned to the room in the large courtyard. We faintly heard the little monk adding another bolt to the star gate in the front.

Film News

A Special Feature The Reason Why the Italian-Abyssinian War Film is Delayed (Part 1) 214

— Lai

Costing More Than 3.3 Million A Total Failure

Before Abyssinia and Italy started the war, the American film industry was already organizing a film news network. The first footage of the Abyssinian Royal Palace and the Abyssinian Emperor's oath was captured by Loichey of Paramount Pictures. Later, Universal Pictures took the lead, uniting several companies, pooling financial and human resources, and assigning groups to undertake the filming work. All war-related areas, even in the remote mountains and forests, were equipped with cameras. The security was stricter than the front lines of both Abyssinia and Italy. However, from the official declaration of war between the two countries to the ceasefire, several months have passed, and such news has not been shown on screens around the world. What exists, such as Paramount Pictures' "Abyssinian Winds," only introduces Abyssinia's internal customs, the Abyssinian Emperor's meetings, military parades, troop movements, and the private lives of important officials. As for the actual combat between the two countries, it is completely absent. Other film companies, such as 20th Century Fox, also independently organized an Abyssinian expedition by Fox-British News Department. Led by Director of Photography Lan Hameng, only fragments of material from the company's newsreels, such as the departure of Italian troops, boarding ships or land travel, and Mussolini's speeches, or the departure of Abyssinian troops, exist to this day. In short, no company has footage of combat scenes in the Italian-Abyssinian news.

Of course, filming real scenes on the battlefield is extremely dangerous. However, when Universal Pictures organized the Italian-Abyssinian war news photography team, it was prepared for all sacrifices, vowing to show the狰狞 face of war to the movie audience. However, the result was a disgrace to the mission. As for why the photography team spent a huge amount of money and manpower, yet the result was nothing?

Manlyn Davies and Dick Bowel Two Protagonists of "Grass Roots"

Great Light Projection

"Carnival Night" Should Not Be Underestimated 215

"Carnival Night" has already completely finished filming. It is one of the national films that will be released after the autumn coolness and has attracted much attention. Shi Dongshan said that dozens of beloved colleagues have put in a lot of effort for this film. If this film receives a lot of praise in the future, the credit belongs to everyone. Indeed, "Carnival Night" shows a very serious attitude in its production, and none of the actors and actresses did not take themselves seriously. Everyone almost forgot everything to engage in the work of this film. For example, Gu Eryi plays a county old man of sixty or seventy years old in "Carnival Night", but he himself is a young man of twenty-two years old. Therefore, every time he films, he arrives six hours earlier than others. This makeup, in the hands of makeup director Xin Hanwen, has to be carefully研磨 for six hours before it can be successful. If he films every day, you can imagine the suffering that Gu Eryi has endured on this. However, Gu Eryi is very excited and very happy, and has never complained, because Gu Eryi has forgotten everything for his work. From this example, thinking about the efforts of everyone else for "Carnival Night" is enough to prove that "Carnival Night" is really not a national film that can be underestimated. Now that the release date is approaching, please pay attention to it.

Star Second Photography Factory Electrician Falls to His Death 216

The company allocates funds for compensation Colleagues offer sacrifices and hold funerals

Wu Xinkang, an electrician at the second photography studio of Pengxing Film Company on Ben Erpei Road, accidentally fell from the awning frame while installing red and green lights outside the photography studio on the morning of the 9th, suffering serious injuries. He was immediately rushed to the Guangci Hospital on Father Jin Road for treatment, but eventually died due to his injuries. It is heard that the Star authorities specially convened a meeting to discuss the aftermath, deeply felt that the worker sacrificed himself on duty, and expressed deep condolences. Today (the 12th) at 2:00 PM, a funeral will be held for him at the Tongren Fuyuan Hall on Ningbo Road, and members from various departments will send祭 and hold a funeral. The coffin will be temporarily placed in the Siming Public Office. As for the worker's family members, in addition to the company allocating funds for compensation, all Star colleagues will also donate to provide comfort.
